vyañjaṃ vyañjaṃ viviśatuḥ saṅgi-gātṛ-kulācale ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] atha sabhāsadaḥ sva-sva-hṛdaya-vihāri maṇimaya-hāri hārādikaṃ dadatas te tu pratyācakhyuḥ-na vayaṃ dravya-vanīyakā nartaka-nāyakāḥ, kintu niyuddha-yācanakā eva, śubhavanto bhavanto malla-tallajā iti varṇanāṃ karṇayoḥ sañcitya niścitya ca samantād vicitya sarvordhvaṃ bhavatāṃ bhavatāṃ samitiṃ samāgatāḥ । atas tad evāsmadīyāya toṣāya poṣāya ca dīyatām, na tu moṣāya nīyatām । [] tad evam avadhārayadbhir eva hasadbhis taiḥ sabhāsadbhir upasarpadbhiḥ saha sahajātau kṛta-śātau tatra-bhavantau tadārabdhavantau । yatra- bhrāmaṇair laṅghanaiḥ kṣepair āsphoṭana-vikarṣaṇaiḥ । []

evaṃ tau loka-siddhābhiḥ krīḍābhiś ceratur vane । nady-adri-droṇi-kuñjeṣu kānaneṣu saraḥsu ca ।।[] [] tad evaṃ sthite dina-katipaye ca prasthite kadācid ahar-mukha eva pūrva-pūrva-pūrvadeva-nirvāpaṇa-bhṛta-nibhṛta-cintā-kṛta-mati-bhraṃśasya kaṃsasya svayam abhyāsaṃ pralamba-nāmā deva-dhrug abhyājagāma । abhyāgamya ca praṇamya vyaktam eva tam anuyuktavān-deva, tava keyaṃ paridevanā balavad āvartamānā dṛśyate? [] pralamba uvāca-bhavatu, mām api yāmam ekaṃ vyāpāraya । kaṃsas tu tuṣṇīm-bhūya dūyamāna-vadanaḥ kṣaṇam āsīt ।
[] pralamba uvāca-deva, katham iva । [] kaṃsaḥ sa-vairasyaṃ vihasya tasya tatra pataṅgatāṃ vibhāvayann uvāca-tvam apy atamasi prajvalaj-jvalana-vartmani vartanīyaḥ । [] pralambaḥ sa-krodham uvāca-aho, sarvaṅkaṣa-jvālasya kālasya mahimā himācalam api jvalayati, yadāśritāṃs taḍāgāṃś ca tāḍayati । [] kaṃsa uvāca-bhavatu yathā bhavad-icchā ।
tāv imau sukumārau ca sarva-mārau kumārau yau । sahasā rahasā yena yena kaṃsād agaṃsātām ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] sarvo' py asau sarva-cālena kālena ghaṭita-kaṭhinatābhyām ābhyāṃ carvita-garvaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ, tad adya samasta-vāsara-visṛmara-vihāra-visaraja-viśvāsa-prapañcanayā vañcayan bandhuvad eva skandha-dvaye hasta-dvaya-kṛta-bandhaṃ dvayam api prakṣipya kṣipram eva bhojarāja-parisaraṃ parisamupahariṣyāmi iti । [] atha sa tu kalkī valkīkṛta-kaccaratādi-pracchanna-sparśa-veśatayā pūrvaṃ goṣṭham āgatya parito dṛṣṭiṃ vitatya veśma-sthita-gopa-bāla-viśeṣa-veṣaṃ samūhya tam eva ca vyūhya miśrī-bhavituṃ śiśrīṣan hasann eva tatra praviṣṭaḥ paridṛṣṭaś ca kṛṣṇena ।
[] dṛṣṭvā ca tac-chalam evāsvaccha-svacchalāyāvalambya-bhadra, kathaṃ vilambam ālambathās, tathāpi bhadraṃ dudyūṣā-samaya eva samayitas tvam asi iti vihasya tad-anukṛta-gopa-bāla-sambandha-viśeṣa-sambandhaṃ parihasya ca bahu-paritoṣitena tena saha sahacaratvaṃ balasya bala-nirjayārtham eva kalayāñcakre । ūce ca-adyārabhya, sabhya, mama parama-suhṛd bhavān eva । tvām aham akṣi-gatatayā sthāpayiṣyāmi । śrīdāmā rāmam evānvetu, sa kila hy antar-vardhana-spardhaḥ spardhana-gaṇam evārhati iti । viśvacikīr api sa vidhiḥ pipaṭhīr yasmād bhavet tasmin । ko vā caturaṃ-manyaḥ prathayatu nija-cāturīṃ kṛṣṇe ।। [upagīti] [] athārbhaka-samudayaṃ vibhāga-dvayam ayaṃ vidhāya taṃ ca pralambaṃ sva-bala-parivṛḍhatayā dṛḍhaṃ nidhāya tatra ca sa-matsaram iva bala-pralambau śrīdāmātmānau mithaḥ pratisaṅghaṭṭinau saṅghaṭayya parān api sajūḥ-kurvāṇatayā tathā praghaṭayā parājitānāṃ ca śatāya parikrītānām api vāhakatvaṃ prakaṭayya saṅgarāya kṛta-saṅgaraḥ sa mādhavo vividha-krīḍā-niviḍamanā babhūva । tataś ca-
tasmin vāhānukartṝṃs turaga-tulanayā hāsayanto hasantaḥ । prāpur bhāṇḍīram ete vanavana-bhuvi gāś cālayantaś calantaḥ ।।[sragdharā] [] tad evaṃ kutūhale tu prabale balaṃ pralamba-skandhārūḍhaṃ sandhātuṃ jita-bhujaga-bhujaḥ śrī-balānujaḥ parābhavam agaṇayan durbalam adurbalam avicitya svīkṛtaṃ svagaṇam eva parābhāvayāmāsa । ūhe kṛṣṇaḥ śrīdāmānaṃ daityaḥ sa śrī-rāmākhyānam ।
anyo' py anyaṃ śūraṃ-manyaḥ sarvaḥ proce dhanyo dhanyaḥ ।।[vidyunmālā] maryādātaḥ paryagāt taṃ pragṛhya ।। [śālinī] taṃ nājñāsīd dṛṣṭa-mātraṃ ca kṛṣṇaḥ । paścād-bhāvī cāturī-sandhurīṇaḥ ।। [śālinī]
[] atha tathāpi giri-nivaha-nibha-vahala-sāratā-vaha-durvaha-svabhāvatā-bhāvita-saṅkarṣaṇa-vapuḥ-karṣaṇa-jāta-dharṣaṇa-vaśān niviḍa-pīḍitatayā vrīḍita-cittatayā ca sa punaḥ punar īḍitaṃ-manyaḥ svam akharvaṃ pūrva-siddhaṃ pūrvadeva-vapur āvirbhāvayāmāsa । śubhra-dhāma-vapuṣaṃ tamaḥ-prabhaḥ । divya-loka-nikaras tv amanyata ।। [rathoddhatā] jyeṣṭhaḥ paśyan drāk kaniṣṭhasya vaktram ।
duṣṭaṃ muṣṭyā tāḍayat suṣṭhu mūrdhni ।। [śālinī] patat tulitam ujjahat pratihari drutaṃ pupluve । tyajan dravati vajrakaḥ sapadi vajra-pāṇiṃ prati ।। [pṛthvī] pralamba-patanaṃ dūre pralambāryāptir antike ।
ubhe te yugapad dṛṣṭe jajñāte smita-vismitī ।। [anuṣṭubh] bāṣpa-śliṣṭatayā tasminn āśliṣṭau bhrātarau mithaḥ । yā vāśliṣyārdratāṃ yātā bandhutā bahir antaram ।। [anuṣṭubh] tadā drutaṃ mṛtavati ca dyavi sthitāḥ ।
vyatarkayann upahasitiṃ harer api ।। [rucirā] vāhaka-śirasi praharaṇam atrādiṣṭaṃ sadā vihṛtau । maryādātikrāntā pralamba bhavatā tathā tu nāsmābhiḥ ।। [udgīti] [] tad evaṃ pralambālambhana-sambhrame' py anudbhrānta-cittās te śṛṅginī-vittāḥ kuṇapatām itasya pramītasya tasya pitṛ-vana-veśaṃ pradeśa-leśaṃ parityajya yojana-vyajya-vistāra-praśasta-bhāṇḍīra-tala-maṇḍalam evādhiṣṭhāya vihāra-niṣṭhāḥ krīḍāpaṇasya spṛhayāyyā jayāyyā gṛhayāyyās tṛṇalobhāviṣṭa-tayā vṛkṣa-ṣaṇḍād viprakṛṣṭām api yamunācchānaccha-muñjāṭavīṃ praviṣṭānām andhī-bhūtānāṃ pāda-bandhanānām anveṣaṇād viśleṣam ājagmuḥ । tataḥ katham apy avadhānataḥ pranaṣṭa-cittatayā spaṣṭa-kaṣṭa-cittā raṃhasā saṅghaśaḥ sabhayaṃ hvayante sma । [] nūnaṃ deśādhipati-nideśataḥ sadeśam āgatā eva kecit krūrā gā dūragā vidadhur iti ca dhyāyanti sma ।
valgūttarīyam anughūrṇya vitīrṇahutau । garjat-taḍid-ghana-ghanāghana-tṛṣṇayeva ।। [vasantatilakā] [] tad evaṃ yadālambhi cāstambhi ca naicikīnicayas tadānīm eva ca dṛṣṭa-nirvilamba-pralamba-pralaya-carāḥ kaṃsa-carā labdhāvasarā muñjāṭavīm udbhaṭa-ceṣṭatayā veṣṭayitvā nirnivāraṇa-kṛpīṭa-kāraṇa-vṛṣṭiṃ jhaṭiti tādṛśa-duṣṭa-vauṣaṭ-kārāspada-tad-vilakṣaṇa-tejasi tasmin pratipakṣatā-kalpanayā nisṛṣṭavantaḥ । [] yā khalu jvāla-kalayāpi sarvaṃ roṣād oṣāmāsa kalpam iti prajvalati mahā-jvalane paṭa-paṭāyamānāyāṃ ca mahā-muñjāṭavyāṃ bhītatayāsta-vyasta-cālās te gopālāḥ sakhi-valayārāmatayā kalita-keli-jālāv iha rāma-gopālāv eva bhūri-dūrataḥ śaraṇatayā samupājagmuḥ । tatra ca-
samīyur vaiyagryaṃ tadapi nija-rakṣām avṛṇuta । tadā śaktiś cāsya prabhavati yathecchaṃ muhur iti ।। [śikhariṇī] kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahā-vīrya he rāmāmita-vikrama । dāvāgninā dahyamānān prapannāṃs trātum arhathaḥ ।।[] ityādi
hā davaṃ prati davaṃ samiyrati । ko yamaḥ ka iha vā bhaved haraḥ ।। [rathoddhatā] [] kintu mayā vaiśvānara-nigaraṇaṃ na soḍhuṃ parivṛḍhā bhaveyur ete iti vicintya provāca-mā bhaiṣṭa netra-puṭaṃ tv anudghaṭitaṃ ghaṭayata iti । [] nimīlad-vilocaneṣu ca teṣu tad-āveśa-vaśayā kṛta-praveśayā yogamāyayā tat-kāla-kalpita-mahā-jaladhara-kalpāpara-śarīras tatratyenānalpenānanena tam aduḥkhata eva sarvaṃ vibhrakṣantaṃ bhakṣitavān ।
[] tathā tad-icchayā sudhā-culukāyamānam ity eke । tayaivaṃ cānyad api cakāra । yad uktaṃ- tataś ca te' kṣīṇy unmīlya punar bhāṇḍīram āpitāḥ । niśāmya vismitā āsann ātmānaṃ gāś ca mocitāḥ ।।iti । [] bala-yuktatayā muralīṃ kalayan ।
vrajam āgatavān ahani glapite ।। [toṭaka] hares tāsāṃ hūtiḥ śravaṇa-gaṇa-bhid-veṇu-raṇitam । na pṛṣṭhyaṃ nāgrīyaṃ na samam avidur na svam api ।। [śikhariṇī] yadyapi bahu-saṅghaṭṭana-dhūli-dhvāntaṃ ca sarvatra ।
tadapi harer mukha-candraḥ pratijanam ānanditaṃ cakre ।। [upagīti] [] atha pūrvavan mātara-pitarādi-racita-sukha-vitarau bhrātarau nija-nilayaṃ praviviśatuḥ । [] sakhāyaś ca pralamba-davānala-kathā-prathanayā sarvaṃ vismāyayāmāsuḥ । īdṛśas tava gopendra putraḥ puṇya-kṛta-stavaḥ । premārdraḥ suhṛdāṃ yas tu dāvāgnim api pītavān ।। [anuṣṭubh]
।। [] pūrva-pūrvānusāreṇa dhenuka-vadhānantara-vyavahāreṇa preyasīnāṃ pratyaham eva vardhamānāḥ kamala-kalikāvad utkalikā madhusūdanasya bahir īhitair durūhāṃ spṛhāṃ bṛṃhayāmāsuḥ । pṛthag loka-dveṣaḥ pratisamayam udvega-kalanā । aho dūra-sthityor api dayitayor eka-rucitā ।। [śikhariṇī]
ādarśāv iva tau svacchau sadābhimukhatāṃ gatau । rādhā-mādhavayor bhāvau mitho bhāvān upeyatuḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] rādhāyāṃ vā śrīharau vā rahas tu । kalyāṇāya prāyaśaḥ kalpate sma ।। [śālinī]
[] tad evaṃ tābhis tasyātidurlabhasya spṛhātiśaya-vāhitayā nātihitāyāṃ śarady ativāhitāyāṃ mārgaśīrṣas tu tāsāṃ patiṃ-manya-gṛha-gamanāya mārga-śīrṣatām avāpa । [] bhavantas tāvat taṭasthī-bhavantas tiṣṭhantu, vayam evāmūr anunīya tat-tad-gṛham upanīya tat-tat-prakriyāṃ kriyā-viṣayī-kariṣyāmaḥ iti । [] atha janyaṃ-manyāṃs teṣām anādaram avadhāya manyuṃ manyamānān svayam eva sā devatādi-mānyā sāmnā sammānya yathā sva-manīṣitam evāṅgīkārayāñ cakāra । [] kanyās tu tā dhanyā varaṃ-manyālayāntaḥ-prayāṇaṃ tatra ca labdha-tad-añcala-nyāsa-nijāñcalatādy-anyāyam asammanyamānā babhūvuḥ ।
[] atha tāḥ sā śapatha-prathanayā tad-ālayeṣv asambhavam apīṣṭa-lambhanam aniṣṭa-vipralambhanaṃ ca viśrambhaviṣayaṃ vidhāya duḥsaha-nānādhyavasāyād viṣkambhya gamana-karmaṇi lambhyamānāḥ pathi tu svamāyayā gopayantī tatra tat-sadṛg-anyāś cāropayantī tat tan nirvāhayāmāsa । paścād eva ca tās tatra vāsayāmāsa । tās tu tatra ca parama-trastā babhūvuḥ, yataḥ- kṛṣṇālābhād gopikānāṃ babhūva । yady evaṃ dhik śvāśuraṃ vahnir eva ।। [śālinī] apy anukūlaṃ yāsāṃ pratikūlaṃ syād vidūrage kṛṣṇe ।
tāsāṃ pratikūlaṃ tu sphuṭam evāsīt kukūla-talpābham ।। [gīti] [] tathāpi paurṇamāsī tās tat-tad-geha-madhyam adhyāsīnā vidhāya yadā calitum udyatāsīt tadāmūḥ punar vica-pracām āptā niśca-pracā-kṛte tad idam ādiṣṭavatī, yadā bhavatībhiḥ sva-maryādā-lopas tarkyate, tadā prapalāyya sthīyatām । samādhānaṃ punaḥ kayācid vidyayāsmābhir eva vidhātavyam, sahasā palāyana-dhāma ca tatra tatra vidhātavyam iti । yāvān ajani nirodhas tāvaty utkāpi saṃvavṛdhe । kṛṣṇa-premavatīṣu śvāsānila-līnatāṃ yātā ।। [upagīti]
yadyapi manasi samiddhā hari-pariripsā tathāpi tābhiḥ sā । āvriyate sma vicārais tatir iva vahneḥ sad-indhana-prakaraiḥ ।। [gīti] bhāva-prāpti-guṇaḥ sadārdra-hṛdayaḥ sad-bhrū-cakorī-gatiḥ । dharmo gacchati kintv adharma-padavīṃ ruddhvā ca māna-kṣayām ।। [śārdūlavikrīḍita]
mad-eka-ceto mat-prāṇā rādhānya-vaśatāṃ gatā । yāṃ smaran mama hā cetaś cetanām āvariṣyati ।। [anuṣṭubh] rādhāṃ tathā smaran kṛṣṇaḥ snigdhaṃ rāgi vilocanam । kiyanty ahāni mārṣṭi sma hanta hāridra-vāsasā ।। [anuṣṭubh]
dharmātikrami cittaṃ katham adhimitraṃ ca tat prakāśate? । iti harir upacita-yuktir yuyoja dūtyāya kevalāṃ dṛṣṭim ।। [gīti] sarasijodara-śrī-muṣā dṛśā । varada nighnato neha kiṃ vadhaḥ? ।।[] iti ।
kṛṣṇasyānyatra dṛk-prāntaḥ sadbhiḥ śāstra-phalaṃ smṛtam । hanta tāsu punaḥ so' yam ebhiḥ śastra-phalaṃ matam ।। [anuṣṭubh] jvālā harer uta tadīya-ramā-gaṇānām । sāgni-dvijālaya ivāgnitatiḥ samiddhā ।। [vasantatilakā]
lokena lokana-kṛte saha mādhavendoḥ । rādhā jayaty uḍuṣu paurṇima-rādhikeva ।। [vasantatilakā] vīkṣāṃ vakra-praṇaya-valitām ardham ardhaṃ vitene । dūre gatvāpy ahaha muralī-saṃvidaḥ saṃvyadhatta ।। [mandākrāntā]
viharaṇaṃ ca te dhyāna-maṅgalam । kuhaka no manaḥ kṣobhayanti hi ।।[] iti । vṛtaṃ vaktrāmbhojaṃ dhana-khura-parāgair valayitam । milat-pāśaṃ yantraṃ madana-racitaṃ bandhum iva tān ।। [śikhariṇī]
vana-ruhānanaṃ bibhrad āvṛtam । manasi naḥ smaraṃ vīra yacchasi ।।[] iti । [] evam aharahar api parasparaṃ spardhayeva vardhamānatayā tāsām utkalikāḥ kalita-madhu-mādhavādhikalā-vyākulatākulatāṃ kalayāmāsuḥ । gopīnāṃ paramānanda āsīd govinda-darśane ।
kṣaṇaṃ yuga-śatam iva yāsāṃ yena vinābhavat ।।[] iti । śakyā kintu sva-kārya-sphuraṇa-padatayā kiñcid uddeśam āptā । tadvat tasyānuṣaṅge yuga-śatam api tad bhāti śaśvat kalābham ।। [sragdharā] kalāpi yadi viśleṣe yugānāṃ śatatāṃ gatā ।
rātrindivīya-saṅkhyāyāṃ tadā śaṅkāmahe vayam ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] evaṃ sāyam-prātikāvalokana-valataḥ katham api nidāghe' pi kṣapite mayūrān madayitnūnāṃ gadayitnūnāṃ ca stanayitnūnāṃ samāgamaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ । yathā- yadā tāsām agre hari-paricitaṃ vṛttam aruṇat । pratīpābhāḥ kṛṣṇa-sphuraṇam adhikaṃ hā vidadhire ।। [śikhariṇī]
santaptir āsāṃ hari-rāginīnām । nirṇītir āsīd viparīta-rītiḥ ।। [indravajrā] antaḥ sphurat-kṛṣṇa-ghanābhir ābhiḥ । svājīvya-varṣānugatāḥ plavādyāḥ ।। [indravajrā]
kalāpām āsur etāsu kalāpāś ca kalāpināṃ । smarārdha-candra-bāṇābhā yatraike bhānti conmukhāḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] ānetuṃ kila yad yad atra vidadhuḥ sarvaṃ ca tat pratyuta । hanta dviṣṭa-suhṛd-daśeyam uditā hā hā vidheḥ kā gatiḥ? ।। [śārdūla]
prāñcad-vṛṣṭija-vāri-vāriṇi taru-kroḍe' śana-krīḍanam । dūrād dhenv-anuhūtir apy aghajitā naś cittam ulluñcati ।। [śārdūla] samasta-jana-śarmadāḥ sapadi khañjarīṭekṣaṇāḥ । hari-vraja-nava-priyās tamasi līnatām āgatāḥ ।। [pṛthvī]
iraṃmada-radās te' mī nīradā api sarvadā । carvanti kṣauṇi-pṛṣṭha-sthān garjanti kila garvataḥ ।। [udgīti] [] aho, citrīyate seyaṃ prema-gati-vaicitrī yatas tādṛśi ca tad-vṛtte kadācid ānukūlya-spṛśīva śrī-rādhā-stutīnām ādhāratā dṛśyate । [] yathā tasyās tat paśyantyā bhāvaneyam- kiyad aho kṛtavaty asi tad vada ।
tulitam āli gatā ramase sadā ।। [drutavilambitā] prasajatī capalā khalu khelati । nahi nahīdam ṛtor guṇa-varṇanam! ।। iti । [drutavilambita?] meghāgama-samaye' sminn adhigata-haritā dṛśāṃ sampat ।
haraye spṛhayasi rādhe nahi nahi śādvala-vibhūtaye dviṣati ।। iti । [udgīti] śikhaṇḍa-cūḍasya sadātiśarmadā । mūrdhnaḥ śikhaṇḍaṃ ca jagāma vismṛtim ।। [upajāti ] svacchatāṃ vidadhatīti cintitam ।
svaṃ dadhe dvi-guṇa-bhāvanāvilam ।। [rathoddhatā] sa-taḍid-vārida-vṛndaṃ nirīkṣya pūrvaṃ yad eva yā taptā । tad apaśyanty api seyaṃ samprati rādhā bhṛśaṃ dūnā ।। [āryā] [] tatra ca rādhā-kṛṣṇayor nakha-lipi-valayita-kisalaya-dala-dvaya-gataṃ padya-dvayaṃ vāyunā parasparaṃ nītam । tad, yathā-
taḍitaḥ puṇya-śālinyaḥ sadā yā ghana-jīvanāḥ । tena sārdham adṛśyanta, nādṛśyanta ca taṃ vinā ।। [anuṣṭubh] āvṛtim ajahād indur vilasati haṃsaś ca nīla-kañjaṃ ca । vṛndāvanam anu hā dhig daivaṃ tat tan na dṛśyate tasyāḥ ।। iti।। [gīti]
daivāt patraṃ śaśvad āśliṣya sāśru । madhye hāraṃ nāyakaṃ nirmimāte ।। [śālinī] aho vikasad-ātmatām agamad āśu tasyām api । sadā malinatām agād iti kim ālibhiḥ sahyatām? ।। [pṛthvī]
āśliṣya sama-śītoṣṇaṃ prasūna-vana-mārutam । janās tāpaṃ juhur gopyo na kṛṣṇa-hṛta-cetasaḥ ।।[] lāvaṇyaṃ tat te ca līlā-vilāsāḥ । viśleṣe tāny eva hālāhalāni ।। [śālinī]
harer gandhavahān sarve jagat-prāṇatayā viduḥ । tad-viyogena tu kṣāmā rāmās tān āśugākhyayā ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] tad evaṃ yadyapy utkaṇṭhāyāḥ parama-kāṣṭhā jātā, tathāpi kācid api kāñcit prati na prakāśayāmāsa । adharmeṇāpi taṃ bhajāni, iti yathā tās tathā kṛṣṇo' pi tatra tā nirvidyā nirvidya khidyate sma । [] kṛṣṇas tūpayāntaram apaśyan netra-vikṣepa-vetra-vikṣepa-vitrastānām api tāsāṃ vaśyatām ayātānām āvaśyaka-tad-bhāvanāya vaṃśī-śaṃsana-viśeṣam abhyasyati sma । [] yathaiva vakṣyate tatra tatra tad evālakṣya tābhiḥ veṇu-vādya urudhā nija-śikṣāḥ iti । []
[] atha prathamatas tan-manā nijāgra-janmanā yugalī-bhūya muralī-kalīm āvartayati sma । [] tatra tu yadā samuddīpita-bhāvāntare vanāntare go-cāraṇe sarva-manaso' py agocarān sahacarān vismāpayann atikānta-guṇa-vrajena nijāgrajena saha svayam aharahaḥ saharṣa utkarṣaṃ pravīṇayan veṇu-śikṣām īkṣayām āsa,।। [] tadā tāsāṃ tad-rūpa-sphūrtir atīva pūrtim āyātā । [] sā ca yathāvad eva, yatas tasya bhāva-vaibhavasya svabhāva evāyam, yad dūrataś ca sva-viṣayaṃ viṣayīkaroti । tathā hi- anumāna-gatā tāsām arthāpattiḥ pratīyate । yataḥ kṛṣṇasya dayitās tā eva nyāya-paṇḍitāḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh]
[] tatra yāḥ punar atīva snigdhatā-digdha-hṛdayās tad duḥkhataḥ śuṣkatām avāpur na tu punaḥ svaka-duḥkhaṃ puṣkalaṃ menire । [] yathā rādhāyā viśākhā lalitā paryāyānurādhā ca, candrāvalyāḥ śaivyā padmā cety-ādayaḥ । tāsu tu tāḥ sva-mātra-niṣṭhatāṃ niṣṭaṅkya svayam eva sa-sauhārdaṃ nija-hārdam āvedayāñcakruḥ । tathāpi tatra prathamaṃ rāma-sahitatā-pihitam eva taṃ lupta-varṇa-padaṃ varṇayāmāsuḥ । rāmo rāmānuja iti yugalam । kṛta-naṭa-veṣatayā paṭu rājati gāyati sakhi-gaṇa-yugalam । [dhruva]
sarasa-rasālaja-pallava-tallaja-pallavitāmala-śīrṣam । nava-yauvana-vana-bījāṅkuram iva dhāvayad-atanu-cikīrṣam ।। vāñchita-piñchāvali-parilāñchita-maṇi-nicayāñcita-keśam । dadhad iva hari-dhanur-anugata-tārā-vali-valitāmbuda-leśam ।।
valayita-nava-dalad-utpala-karṇika-karṇa-yugādbhuta-śobham । latikā kāsāv iti vismayakṛti madhukṛti vinihita-lobham ।। hasta-kamalam abhi kamala-vighūrṇana-ramaṇa-kalā-ramaṇīyam । madhupa-gaṇaṃ prati madhu-kaṇa-varṣaṇam akṛta yataḥ kamanīyam ।।
mālāmālā-parimala-bali-bali-vapur ali-valita-sadeśam । ali-jhaṅkṛti-nuti-kolāhala-vaha-bahula-kutūhala-veśam ।। sitam asitaṃ vapur asitaṃ pītaṃ vasanaṃ yasya ca gītam । tad idaṃ yadi gokulam anu gokulam ayati tadāgham atītam ।। ।। ।
gobhiḥ sākaṃ sakhi-valayitaṃ dṛśyate bhrātṛ-yugmam । dīptiḥ kiñcin nigamana-kalāśāli netraṃ ca tatra ।। [mandākrāntā] saṅgāyato viharato harataś ca tasya । hārāṇi-netram anu vidhyati mānasaṃ naḥ ।। [vasantatilakā]
sā kila kulajā kulajā nayane tasyāḥ paraṃ nayane । veṇu-vinodī madanaḥ sa bhavati yasyāḥ svayaṃ madanaḥ ।। [upagīti] [] tad evam aghadamanena tāsāṃ krama-paramparātaḥ parasparaṃ sva-viṣayābhilāṣa-vyañjanā-sañjanaṃ kiñcil lajjā-paryayam ācarya tādṛśa-ramya-sva-vidyā-bala-tāratamya-viduratayā vidūrato' pi tam avadhārya para-parataḥ parārdhyaṃ samardhyamānāṃ punar veṇu-śikṣāṃ vilakṣaṇī-kurvatā saṅkarṣaṇaḥ kevalaṃ lakṣyāya kalpayāñcakre । yatra hi sarvam eva yugapan mugdhatā-digdhaṃ babhūva । nānāraṇyaṃ prati viharator bibhrator yaṣṭi-rajjū ।
bhrātror āsīd bata tanu-bhṛtāṃ dharmato vaiparītyam ।। [mandākrāntā] nūnam evaṃ vidadhatoḥ sarveṣāṃ dharma-paryayam । kṛṣṇo' mūlam asau cāsmad-dharmam unmūlayiṣyati ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] tad evaṃ bhrātṛbhyāṃ saṅgāne yugapad eva sarveṣāṃ mohanam ūhamānenānujena vicāritam-[] hanta tāsām eva mohanākarṣaṇe suṣṭhu mamābhīṣṭe, tatrāpi rādhābhidhāyāḥ । tasmāt pṛthag bhavan pṛthag eva yathā jīvānāṃ jātir yathā-yuktaṃ tayor dvayam ekaṃ vā vahati, kramaśo vyaktir api, tathā śikṣārthaṃ prayatiṣye । tac ca tat-tan-mātrātiśayitābhīpsita-svarādi-marma-samudbhāvanayā sambhaviṣyati iti ।
[] tad evaṃ vicārayatā tena parīkṣā-paryālocanārtham uttaram uttarāṃ vaśyatām atītatarāṇy avarāṇi sattvāni kramaśaḥ sva-vaśatām ānītāni, tathāpi tat-preyasībhiś citta-kṣobha-mātraṃ tu lebha eva । pibaty etāṃ gavyā yad anu rasanā-karṇa-yugalam । kim etat kiṃ naitad bhavati kim ivaitat kim iti vā ।। [śikhariṇī] yadapy eṣā jātā tadapi kila bhedo vilasati ।
vayaṃ naitad vidmaḥ kva bhavati yuge tasya kalanam ।। [śikhariṇī] vaṃśaḥ so' yaṃ tu vītaṃsaḥ kaṃsa-śatror itīyate । tena śaṃsanato yānti vidhvaṃsaṃ mṛga-pakṣiṇaḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] śrīmān kṛṣṇo viharati padāmbhoja-lakṣmīṃ vitanvan ।
vanyāḥ sarve yayur iti sadā raṅgatāṃ yaj jagāma ।। [mandākrāntā] yad barhyādyāś ca bhānti pratipada-sukṛta-prodayād asmad-arhyāḥ । te tasya svairam īkṣāṃ vidadhati na tad-ābhāsam aṇv apy ayāma ।।[sragdharā] [] atha dināntare' pi tebhyo vicchidya hariṇyas tathā kṛtāḥ । tac ca pūrvavat tābhir varṇitam-
jātyā mūḍham api vyatītya bhavatīr apy evam īhāṃ dadhe । tasyāpy arcanam ullasat-praṇayatas tatrāpi netrāñcalaiḥ ।। [śārdūla] tathā bhartāras tat-praṇaya-naya-siddha-vraja-bhuvaḥ । dhig asmān duṣpuṇyā dadhima nahi tāsām api tulām ।। [śikhariṇī]
kṛṣṇas tu tad-gurur iti pratataṃ pratīmaḥ । mauna-vratena śṛṇuyuḥ parito niviṣṭāḥ ।। [vasantatilakā] yasmād asau munis te ca munayaḥ sarvataḥ sthitāḥ । tasmāt kāñcit spṛhām atra nāñcitāṃ kartum arhatha ।। [anuṣṭubh]
devyo rūpa-vilāsa-mohana-kalām āsādya mohaṃ gatāḥ । veti srastam abhūt kacādi kim u vā naivety api prāyaśaḥ ।। [śārdūla] hanta devyo' pi yatraitām avasthām āpur añjasā । tadīya-vraja-bhū-bālā varākyas tatra kā vayam? ।। [anuṣṭubh]
[] tad evaṃ cetanāṃs tathā vitatha-cetanān vidhāyācetanān api cetanān ivācaritum ārabhate sma । acala-maryādayā paryāptāḥ sphuṭam amūr ākraṣṭum acetanatām atikramyāpi duḥśakā iti । phullat-pūratayā sphurad-ghana-rasā haṃsādi-gīḥ-śiñjitāḥ । bhaṅgālola-bhujaiḥ saroja-valayas tasyāṅghri-yugmaṃ dadhuḥ ।। [śārdūla] taṃ vidrutya milanti ced ahaha kā dīnās tadānīṃ vayam? ।
svalpāpīti nivṛttir eva sukhato yuktāthavā duḥkhataḥ ।। [śārdūlavikrīḍitam] svasādṛśyāt kintu vyatikṛta-hitatvād api sadā । sa cāyaṃ chāyābhiḥ praśamayati tāpaṃ tad-upari ।। [śikhariṇī] cchāyābhiḥ svarasaiś ca taṃ paricaraty antaścara-premataḥ ।
gaṇyās tasya vinā tu sevanam amūr jīvāma dhig jīvitam ।। [sragdharā] kṛṣṇe rameṇa yasmāt tam anu muralikā-vādanāyādhirūḍhe । sarvāṅgīna-dravair apy anuga-sakhi-dhanaṃ sevate taṃ cirāya ।। [sragdharā] citraṃ cen na pratītir bhavati kila girau dṛśyatāṃ cāparatra ।
āgād yatrāsti sākṣi pratipadam uditaṃ kṛṣṇa-mukhyāṅghri-cihnam ।।[sragdharā] tathāpy anugatis teṣāṃ bhāti ced asti dṛṣṭatā ।। [anuṣṭubh] gopīnāṃ svam api hriyaṃ pariharan śaśvat pibann ardati । yad-vaṃśyā naga-jātayo' pi madhubhir bāṣpaṃ madād bibhrati ।। [śārdūla]
tṛṣṇag-bhāvena sajjan bahu-ruci viharan durlabhaḥ syāt paratra । tena jñāyeya seyaṃ mama viraha-dutā dārutām āgateti ।। [sragdharā] āsyaṃ prekṣi tathāṅgam aṅgam asakṛn māle tvam āliṅgasi । hā tat-tad-vidhi-bhāg-vicāra-hatakenābhīpsitād vañcitāḥ ।। [śārdūla]
aho sumanaso muktā vajrāṇy api harer uraḥ । na tyajanti vayaṃ tatra kā vā smara-vaśāḥ striyaḥ? ।। [anuṣṭubh] śyāma eṣa na tu tarhi dunomi । saṅginaḥ katham idaṃ kalayāmi ।। iti । [svāgatā]
[] tad etat-paryantam antara-sparśi-rāga-parīte tasya veṇu-gīte ko' pi sambhramaḥ sarvam eva vrajaṃ nighnaṃ kurvan vighnam ācarati sma । [] sa tu prātaḥ prastoṣyate । ity añjaliṃ baddhvā punar uvāca- asya tvadīya-kāntasya rādhe jānāti ko' pi na । prayāsābhyantara-sthāyi-tvan-nimitta-prayāsatām ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] tad evaṃ kathāyāṃ samāpta-prathāyāṃ sarve yathā sva-svāvāsam āsannāḥ ।
।। mahā-prabhāveṣu vibhāta-paṅktiṣu । sa snigdhakaṇṭhaḥ kathayāmbabhūva ca ।। [upajāti ] [] atha tasminn āśvināvaśeṣe labdha-viśeṣe yajña-yogya-veśe vrajād bahiḥ pradeśe sarva eva parvaṇā sāndrānanda-vrajā iva sa-prajāḥ vrajendrādayaḥ sambhrāntāśaya-prāyatayā carantaḥ surendra-yāga-yogam ācarantaḥ sthānādi-sañceṣkriyamāṇān ādiśantaḥ sva-sva-vasatiṃ vihāya vasatiṃ bahir vasanti sma ।
[] tadā ca kadācid ekasyāṃ sandhyāyāṃ gocāraṇa-bhū-bhāgataḥ samāgataḥ saṅkarṣaṇa-sahacāritayā labdha-harṣaḥ sa-kutuka-tṛṣṇaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇas tadīya-caritam ālocitavān । tatraiva ca prabhūta-kutukākuta-sambhūtatayā vasati sma । [] tad api ca yad api pūrva-pūrva-saṃvatsareṣu dṛṣṭam ity apūrva-dṛṣṭaṃ na bhavati, tathāpi samprati prauḍhatāprakāśataḥ śatamanyuṃ prati manyuṃ janayan janakādiṣu praṇaya-kopaṃ jñāpayann ajñānata iva jijñāsāñcakre । yadyapi śataparva-pāṇir evaṃ garvāyate, ete gopālana-kārakāḥ ke varākāḥ? nikhila-loka-lokapāla-pālakasya mama dakṣa-mukhyāḥ prajāpatayaḥ svīya-manvantara-pati-prabhṛtayaḥ pṛthivī-patayaḥ kamalajanma-janma-pradhānā munīśānā yajamānā virājantetarām iti, tathāpy ete mat-pitṛ-puraḥ-sarās tatra bhaktim atiriktīkurvanti iti । kathyatāṃ vaḥ pitaḥ ko' yaṃ sambhramaḥ samupāgataḥ? । yajñārtho yadi devaḥ kaḥ? pramāṇaṃ kiṃ, phalaṃ ca kim? ।। [anuṣṭubh]
yathā vidhātuṃ bhavatāṃ tathā śrotuṃ ca naḥ spṛhā । ubhayeṣāṃ yatas tatra viśeṣāśrayatā-sthitiḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] atha, kim asmābhir vyaktaṃ vaktavyaṃ gotrabhit-satraṃ prati, kiṃ vāyaṃ vatsaḥ pratipatsyete iti vicikitsati tāta-pāde tad eva kiñcid atiriktaṃ vyaktam iva kartum icchati sma । [] yathā ca, tāta, sarvatra nipuṇānāṃ vaijñānikānāṃ bhavatāṃ putrā vayaṃ na tāvad gocārakatā-mātra-paryavasita-paryālocanāḥ, kintu kiñcit kiñcij jñāna-nītiṃ dharma-rītim api pratipadyāmahe iti vyañjanayā mañju vadati sma- tasmin jīvāḥ santi naivātibhinnāḥ ।
tasmād eṣāṃ gopanaṃ naiva yuktam ।। [śālinī] yogināṃ matam etac cen nītir apy avadhāryatām । udāsīno' rivad varjyaḥ suhṛd ātmaiva sammataḥ ।। yady eṣa panthā dharmasya so' pi nāsty avicārataḥ । tatra yad viduṣaḥ siddhir bhaven nāviduṣaḥ kvacit ।। dharmo vaidika eveṣṭau laukikaḥ kvāpi dṛśyate ।
bhavadbhiḥ kas tayor eṣa viśeṣatvena sammataḥ? ।। [anuṣṭubh] dharmo' yaṃ laukikas tāta yadyapi syād athāpy asau । yuktatvād api cāmnāyād āmnāyaja iveṣyate ।। ya indro devatātra syāt parjanyaḥ sa tu sarvavit । tasyārcanaṃ kulāyātam asmākaṃ ketanaṃ matam ।। [anuṣṭubh]
svataḥ karma-vaśād evādātuṃ karmānusāriṇaḥ । īśaś ced asti karmānugāmy asau kā nu devatā ।। sarvaṃ tad bhasmani hutaṃ para-tantre yad arpaṇam । gārhapatye hutaṃ tat tu yad ātmātmīya-poṣaṇam ।। tasmād ābhīra-vaiśyatvād aghnyāsevā tu naḥ kṛtiḥ । devatā yadi manyeta mantavyā sā tad-āśrayā ।। [anuṣṭubh]
rajo-bhūr yavasādy-arthas tasmān nendro gavāśrayaḥ । kintu govardhanākhyāna-kṣauṇī-bhṛd yaḥ sa eva saḥ ।। nijājīvyatayā gāvaḥ kulāgatyā ca bhū-surāḥ । āśrayatve samakṣatvaṃ yānty ete na divaukasaḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] āptavāg anumānaṃ ca pratyakṣād eva gamyate ।
tasmāt pratyakṣam eva syāt pramāṇaṃ sarva-mardakam ।। tasmād gavāṃ brāhmaṇānām adreś cārabhyatām mahaḥ । aindrair nirmīyatāṃ seyaṃ tri-karmī haviṣāṃ kulaiḥ ।। homo yadi vidhātavyo vahnim uddiśya hūyatām । āśrayaḥ sa hi sarveṣāṃ pratyakṣaś cānubhūyate ।। atha viprāḥ prīṇanīyā dattvā dhenūḥ sadakṣiṇāḥ । svabhāva eṣa bhavatāṃ vidhi-kiṅkaratā nahi ।। [anuṣṭubh]
ebhyaḥ śvabhyo' py atra gobhyas tṛṇāni । yasmād eṣo' py anna-kūṭābhidhaḥ syāt ।। [śālinī] vipraṃ vahniṃ gāṃ parikrāmatādrim । svacchandatvād yānam apy atra diṣṭam ।। [śālinī]
ye vā kratubhujo' py atra janās te syur janāv iha । suparvāṇaḥ sumanaso nirjarāś ca surā iva ।। [anuṣṭubh] āḍhyaṅ-karaṇī subhagaṅ-karaṇī tadvat priyaṅ-karaṇī । śrī-govardhana-pūjā-nāmnī vidyā parisphurati ।। [upagīti]
govardhana-giri-yajñāvajñā tu gotrabhit-pūjā । andhaṅ-karaṇī palitaṅ-karaṇī nagnaṅ-karaṇy api ca ।। [upagīti] go-viprādi-prepsitaṃ mad-dhitaṃ ca । kāryaṃ vighnaḥ syād vibhinna-praveśe ।। [śālinī]
yuṣmadṛgbhiḥ sādhyate kāyikaṃ vā । tasmād etan mad-dhitatvād vidheyam ।। [śālinī] anunmattaḥ svataḥ sarvaṃ vetti svīyaṃ hitaṃ pitaḥ । no ced vetti na ca brūte brūte ced vetti niścitam ।। [anuṣṭubh]
[] tad etad vipralambha-lambhanam apy akliṣṭa-varṇana-viśiṣṭam ākarṇya tan-mukhaṃ ca nirvarṇya, tad eva savarṇair asavarṇair apy adhi parvam āgataiḥ sarvakair nirṇinye । tathā hi- sarveṣāṃ tad yāti nūnaṃ ruciṃ ca । vācyaṃ tasmāt te' py amanyanta tadd hi ।। [śālinī] [] tad etad avadhārya madhukaṇṭhas tv amukta-kaṇṭhaṃ parāmṛśati sma, ced apy ativedaḥ suvicāratā-naśvaraḥ so' yam anīśvara-vādaḥ kṛta-vakra-bhāva-cakra-śakra-parābhava-kautuka-tātparya-mātra-pātratayā tena prayuktaḥ, kintu na pravṛtti-virodhi-pātratayā; tathāpi tatra mitratāticitratayā labdha-nigama-visrabdha-sarva-puruṣārtha-sārtha-śiromaṇi-rūpa-svarūpeṣu teṣu vraja-bhūpeṣu nāyuktaḥ । īśvara-jñāna-gurubhir api tad-bhāvam eva pari sarvopari-purutā-parāmarśāt । yathoktam-
aho bhāgyam aho bhāgyaṃ nanda-gopa-vrajaukasām । yan-mitraṃ paramānandaṃ pūrṇa-brahma sanātanam ।।[] ityādi । [] tataḥ kautuka-cāritayāpi tena yad vicāritam iva sampadyate, tad api pāramārthya-varyatayā paryavasyatīty evam aho parama-maho-vara-kara-svabhāva-dhāraḥ so' yaṃ vraja-dharā-pati-vaṃśa-janmā śaśadharaḥ iti । [] snigdhakaṇṭha uvāca-tataś ca dīpāvalīnāmānam amāvāsyām anu dīpāvali-bali-kautukaṃ pratipadya pratipat-prātas tu viśrambhataḥ paramāśrayatām āśrayamāṇair amībhir yathā tena vihitaṃ tathā vihitam ।
[] tatra ca mukhya-kalpa-kalpanāya vicitra-citra-vitāna-patākādibhiḥ sarva-sukha-saṃvardhanasya śrī-govardhanasya kūṭa-maṇḍalaṃ maṇḍayitvā, yathāvidhi nirbandha-sādhita-sādhu-gandha-bandhura-pādyādi-prāgrya-sāmagrībhir abhisabhājya, tam abhi prājya-caraṇācalavad ājya-prāghāra-nirjharāś citra-varṇa-vyañjana-vyañjita-dhātu-rañjanāḥ, dugdha-taṭinī-saṅkaṭitā dadhi-taḍāga-saṅghaṭitāḥ sampannam anna-kūṭāḥ saṅghaṭṭayya nikaṭād upaḍhaukayāmāsire । yeṣāṃ prāg-bhāvenāpūpikaṃ śāṣkulikam ityādi bhūyiṣṭha-niṣṭhāna-kūṭa-nāmnā sthānāny api ciram āmnātāni । svargaṃ bāḍhaṃ vyānaśe tatra satre । nirṇinyāte karṇa-śūle nidānam ।। [śālinī] kṛṣṇākāraḥ kaścid āvirbabhūva ।
yasmāt kṛṣṇe kāraṇatvaṃ jagāma ।। [śālinī] kiṃ vā dhātu-dyoti-bhūbhṛd vibhāti? । mūrti-vyūhaḥ sphūrtim atrātanoti? ।। [śālinī] vistāra-dyutimanti veṣamaṇayaḥ sūryādi-jetṛ-prabhāḥ ।
yasya kṣmādhara-deva eṣa kurute netrāṇi citrāṇi naḥ ।। [śārdūla] [] tataḥ sa tu caturānana-cāturī-cālana-caturaḥ kṛṣṇa-nāmnā madhuraḥ sa-praśrayaṃ papraccha-bhagavan, ko bhavān? iti । [] devas tu nirghoṣa-nibha-ghargharita-svareṇābhra-bhramaṃ prathayann, arthena tu tam anyathayan vacaḥ pracārayām āsa, pūrvitākharvavat-parvan! parvataḥ so' yam aham asmi iti । [] tad etad avadhārya devāry-amitraḥ śrīdāmādi-mitraḥ sva-bhujau prasārya visphūryamāṇa-kolāhalānargalaṃ gopa-vargaṃ nivārya, namaskāryaḥ khalv asau yasmāt karuṇā-vyagratā-jāgran-mahā-vigraha-samagra-vigraha-prakāśa-grahilatayā pratyakṣa-pratyayam eva sa eva devaḥ pratyavaruddhavān iti sarvān praty akharvāṃ vācam uvāca ।
[] uktvā cākhaṇḍa-daṇḍavan-natiṃ kurvati sahasa-smita-pūrvaje tasmin vismita-manasaḥ sarva eva prati parvataṃ tathākurvata । kṛtvā ca śraddhayā baddhāñjaliṣu tadāvaliṣu sarva-sukha-vardhanaḥ sa govardhanaḥ punar uvāca- bhedaṃ yuṣmad vicakṣmahe । pratyakṣaṃ bhuṅkṣmahe vayam ।। [anuṣṭubh] apy eṣa pratikūṭam eka-kavala-prāptānnam ādat tathā ।
kuṇḍāny āśu sarāṃsi kiṃ ca sarito ninye kṣayaṃ sarvataḥ ।। [śārdūla] yadā grāsāya sa karaṃ prasārayati cāgrataḥ । tadā sarve dravanti sma sarvataś caṭakā iva ।। [anuṣṭubh] grāsaṃ grāsaṃ pāṇinā dakṣiṇena ।
śakraṃ lolat-prānta-gatyā jahāsa ।। [śālinī] cākuñce ca sthagita-haritaḥ prāpta-tat-tad-gatīnām । yat kvāpy ekaṃ na kila gaṇitaṃ siktham ekaṃ sthitaṃ na ।। [mandākrāntā] atarītṛṇyata grāsān bhūbhṛd-bhūbhṛd yathā yathā ।
acalīklpyatāpy uccair māṃsalāya tathā tathā ।। [anuṣṭubh] hāsaṃ vṛddhāś citram arhās tu bhaktim । śuddhāṃ tuṣṭiṃ kautukitvād babhāja ।। [śālinī] vaktraṃ śaśvat kṣālayann adridevaḥ ।
vṛṣṭiṃ kurvan śampa-sṛṣṭiṃ cakāra ।। [śālinī] dantāntargāny anna-piṇḍāni kuñcan । pūrtiṃ kurvan prāṇa-bhājāṃ sasarja ।। [śālinī] kūṭī-kurvaṃś carvayan garva-phullaḥ ।
prātar yadvat tadvad āsyaṃ cakāra ।। [śālinī] tasmin drāghīyasi syāt katham iti vividhād dhvasta-cittā vicārāt । yasmin dīpāḥ sahasraṃ talam upari ca te cālyamānā virejuḥ ।। [śārdūla] [] atha sarvam icchan anvicchan pratīcchann api girir ayam aho giriṃ karotīti nidhyāya, mūrdhani baddhāñjalitayā sarvasminn apy ūrdhvaṃ sthitavati, sarvato' pi varān varān viracayyātarkitam antarhite parama-hite tasminn, akhaṇḍa-daṇḍavat-praṇāma-pūrvam atra dvitra-kṣaṇaṃ citram iva sarva evāsīt ।
vahat-prakaṭatāṃ bhajann akhilam eva bhuṅkte sma saḥ । purandara-bali-grahād atibalī tathā tarkyate ।। [śikhariṇī] [] tataś ca sarvo' pi visrabdhaḥ parama-prema-bhājana-go-sabhājanam ārabdhavān । yat khalu- tatra śrī-nanda-rājaḥ svayam ayam upamā tatra tatrāsya putraḥ ।
kiṃ varṇyāḥ kintu nirvarṇanam anu paramaṃ jñeya-bhāvaṃ prayānti ।। [sragdharā] vatsaiḥ pṛktāḥ pramodaṃ pṛthutaram abhajan dhenavaḥ satyam eva । kecid yadvad bhajante madhura-vidhurataḥ saṃskṛtaṃ ṣāḍavādi ।।[sragdharā] rūpya-saṃvṛta-khurā dhṛta-hārāḥ ।
naicikī-nicitayo rucim āñcan ।। [svāgatā] [] tatra gopāḥ śrī-gopālādi-gopāla-satkṛti-camatkṛtim adhigamya, vidhim anugamya, citrakāṅga-nibha-citrātiramya-vastrāvṛtāṅgatayā tarṇakam ākramya, kautukato gāḥ sambhramya, taj-jāta-hāsa-kolāhalād viramya, grāsa-viśrāṇanena tā viśramya, parikramya, praṇamya, cācaryaṃ vāryam ācarya, vitāna-vitānenāgniṃ paricarya, pradakṣiṇāvartatayā vartamānaṃ ca taṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ viracayya, bhūṣaṇa-nivaha-mahitānāṃ purohitādīnāṃ pūjanam api pūrayāmāsuḥ । ścaryaṃ tatra muhuś ca toṣa-rahitās tat-tat-parīvartataḥ । tātāmbādi-tadīya-bāndhava-janā nāntaṃ cirād aiyaruḥ ।। [śārdūla]
yathā kṛṣṇas tathā rāmo rāmo yadvat tathā sa ca । vrajeśayor nātra bhedas tan-mitreṣv api tad-dṛśoḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] gavāṃ, tadā tā nija-vatsa-kṛṣṭitaḥ । yāty eṣa yānti sma tadā tad-ātmatām ।। [upajāti ]
dantair ākarṣakāṃs tān vyathayitum abhito dhāvanārtā yadā syuḥ । jīyād udbhāsa-hāsa-drava-madhu parito mādanaṃ yad vavarṣa ।। [śārdūla] hastāmbhoja-spṛṣṭam īṣat kuruṣva । gāvaḥ suṣṭhu prītitaḥ svādayante ।। [śālinī]
go-rodhanāya paśupā nahi tatra śekuḥ । āsīd alaṃ yad asakau guṇa-koṭi-kalpā ।। [vasantatilakā] na bhavati bata bahulānām atibahulānāṃ parikramaḥ sadyaḥ । ity ekasyā vyakteḥ kriyatāṃ yasmād aśeṣagā jātiḥ ।। [gīti]
tatra pradakṣiṇī-kāryam ekaṃ vṛddhaṃ gavaurasam । mūlārādhanataḥ sarvārādhanaṃ vibudhair matam ।। [anuṣṭubh] śrī-nanda-lokas tu tato' pi goṣu । yogeśa-durgā-namanākhya-bhaktiḥ ।। [indravajrā]
[] ācārya-varaṇa-lakṣaṇam api vilakṣaṇam eva tatra । yataḥ- svayam āvriyatācāryas tatra nādyavad arthitaḥ । yatra suṣṭhu sitaṃ yaṣṭuś cittaṃ tatraiva tasya ca ।। [anuṣṭubh] govardhana-mahā-yajñe hutabhug-vyājatas tadā ।
hareḥ pratāpa evendhāñcakre śakra-pratāpanaḥ ।। yadāgnir dakṣiṇāvarto yajñe jajñe tadā janaḥ । sarvaś ca dakṣiṇāvarta-parīvartam avartata ।। [anuṣṭubh] prakārālaṅkāraṃ sakalam idam apy uttamatamam । mudāvādīd yasmin dada dada damātraṃ vrajapatiḥ ।। [śikhariṇī]
divya-dātavya-sambhāre vraja-rājena yojite । parīkṣakās tatra paraṃ tat-parīkṣakatāṃ yayuḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] yad anu sarve' pi prāṇinaḥ prīṇate sma । tathā hi vandi-jana-vandanam, arthena goduhān nandād arthena ca sadārthinām ।
vadānyaś ca vadānyaś ca vadānyaḥ ko bhaved ataḥ? ।। [anuṣṭubh] sarva-prāṇa-bhṛtāṃ tathāpi hṛdayaṃ nāpūri tatrāṇv api । paśyāścaryam athāpi hanta gatavān saṅkrandanaḥ śuṣkatām ।। [śārdūla] [] atha tad evaṃ vipratrākṛta-satrādikaḥ purohita-hita-sahitaḥ śrī-vraja-yuva-rāja-mahitaḥ sa khalu vijñānāṃ samājaḥ puraskṛta-vraja-rājas tad-yajñāvaśiṣṭaṃ param aviśiṣṭam annam upabhujya, veśa-viśeṣaṃ saṃyujya, gīta-nibaddhaṃ sa-śraddhatayā hari-caritaṃ prati rasan hasan, viśvasan, lasan, parito govardhanaṃ paricakrāma ।
dvijāṃś ca bhojayāmāsuḥ śataśo' tha sahasraśaḥ । gāvaḥ śailaṃ tataś cakrur arcitās tāḥ pradakṣiṇam ।। svāminaḥ parijanā guru-striyaḥ । śreṇi-mukhya-janatāś ca cakramuḥ ।। [rathoddhatā]
vādyādi-prakaṭana-dhīvarā naṭādyāḥ । tanvānāḥ punar iha dhīvaratvam āpuḥ ।। [praharṣiṇī] giri-pūjeyaṃ vihitaṃ kena? araci śakra-padam abhayaṃ yena । giri-pūjeyaṃ vihitaṃ kena? pūtanikā sā nihatā yena ।।
giri-pūjeyaṃ vihitaṃ kena? tṛṇāvarta-tanu-dalanaṃ yena । giri-pūjeyaṃ vihitaṃ kena? yamalārjuna-tarum udakali yena ।। giri-pūjeyaṃ vihitaṃ kena? vatsa-bakāsura-hananaṃ yena । giri-pūjeyaṃ vihitaṃ kena? vyomāghāsura-maraṇaṃ yena ।।
giri-pūjeyaṃ vihitaṃ kena? kāliya-damanaṃ kalitaṃ yena । giri-pūjeyaṃ vihitaṃ kena? khara-pralambaka-śamanaṃ yena ।। giri-pūjeyaṃ vihitaṃ kena? dava-yugmaṃ paripītaṃ yena । giri-pūjeyaṃ vihitaṃ kena? trasyati kaṃsaḥ satataṃ yena ।। [।।]
mano-haraṇam āvahan vraja-nivāsināṃ sarvataḥ । jaḍīkṛta-śarīratā bhavati taṃ tu kālaṃ vinā [।।] [śikhariṇī] tāsāṃ gopa-tatīr vidhāya sakhibhiḥ sārdhaṃ hariḥ sāgrajaḥ । kanyā-kuṅkuma-yuk-karāṅka-vilasat-pṛṣṭhaḥ sphurad-veṣavān ।। [śārdūla]
gṛhṇaṃś ca pratikūla-gāmi-dhavalā vidrutya saṅkocayan । kurvan vādita-valgu-veṇu-paritaś cakrāma govardhanam ।। [śārdūla] cakāra mandaṃ laghu vā yadṛcchayā । tatrāyayuḥ sūtra-niyantritā iva ।। [upajāti ]
[] tad evaṃ bahula-kutūhalataś cālaṃ cālam amī gopa-grāmaṇyas tad eva ramyaṃ yajña-dhāma samāgamya paramānandād vāṇinī-prabhṛti-kṛta-nṛtya-vādya-gīta-grāmiṇīṃ yāminīṃ viśrāmyanti sma । prātaś ca dvitīyāyām ahimakara-kanyāyā mahima-śravaṇataḥ praṇatatayā tasyāṃ snānam ācarya nikāyyam evāgacchanti sma । [] tasyāṃ ca bhrātṛ-dvitīyāyāṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ praśastena bhaginī-hastena bhoktavyam iti parama-dhanyābhir upanandādi-kanyābhir mitho milantībhir nimantritau praṇaya-yantritau tatra sa-tṛṣṇau ca rāma-kṛṣṇau sahacara-nikareṇa saha bhojana-kareṇa saha maham arocayatām । [] tad evaṃ vṛtte vṛtte, kṛṣṇasya samunnaddhatā-bandhayā kuhanayā mad-yajña-pratyūhanam idam ity ūhamānaḥ śakras tu vakra-bhāva-cakratayā cukrodha । [] kṛṣṇena tasya yā gūḍhāpi khaṭvārūḍhatā tarkitā, sā katham anyathā samparkitayā varteteti vyaktīkartum iva matsaratas tat-sahita-viśva-mahita-śrīman-nandādi-nindā-pūrvakaṃ saṃvartaka-meghān vraja-vighātāya pravartayāmāsa । tataś ca- śampā-nirghoṣa-vīpsā-spṛg iti paśu-kule goṣṭham evāśu nīte ।
tan-nirdeśāt tam ādriṃ sapadi parigatās tasthur ūrdhvaṃ nirīkṣya ।।[sragdharā] indro yadi mahā-vṛṣṭiṃ naṣṭa-sṛṣṭiṃ taniṣyati । tad-aṅgīkāri-girirāṭ kṛpāṃ sāṅgīkariṣyati ।। [anuṣṭubh] kaṭhora-kuṭha-kuṭṭakaiḥ kuṭila-vāyubhiḥ kuṇṭhite ।
jane prakaṭam āṭa sā prathita-dhṛṣṭi-vṛṣṭi-prathā ।। [pṛthvī] vajratvaṃ bata vajra-pāta-nicayāḥ sūrya-prapāta-bhramam । haste' dhatta yathā na kena ca tadā śaktaṃ darāpy ūhitum ।। [śārdūla] svāntān medūra-mānī tad amum anu mayā māna-bhaṅga-prasaktaḥ ।
mac-citte sāvaśeṣaṃ tad idam atha mayā prāṇa-sāmyena dhāryam ।। iti । samajani halinā na harer giri-dhṛti-sambhrama-vaśena saṃvādaḥ । tad api paraspara-hārdā- jñānaṃ tasminn ajījanat tam iva ।। [gīti] [] yatra khalu muhur api he-śabdaḥ plutatāpluta evāsīt । tathā hi-amba he, mā vilambasva । tāta he, atraiva yūyam āyāta । ārya he, sarvān ādāyāgaccha iti prabhṛti ।
praśāmya suhṛdāṃ tate mama tu ko' pi nātra śramaḥ । samutpatana-līlayā sa varivarti tūla-prabhaḥ ।। [pṛthvī] sthānaṃ paśyann asmi pātāla-kalpam । saṅgātīte no nipatyādi cātra ।। [śālinī]
mātar mantraṇayā mā māṃ nivartayata sattamāḥ । udasto yena tad-dhastād dhvastaḥ syād girirāṭ katham? ।। [anuṣṭubh] mā vilambadhvam atyarthaṃ yuṣmad-duḥkhena kampratām । mayi gacchaty adripatiḥ patitā viśata drutam ।। [anuṣṭubh]
drutam aviśan nikhilas tadādri-garte । sa bhajati kintu tad-eka-tarṣi-buddhyā ।। [puṣpitāgrā] maṇi-śreṇi-vidyotamāna-pradeśam । tad-ūrdhvaṃ ca tat-tūlya-śobhā-pracāram ।। [bhujaṅgaprayātā]
samastāvakāśārha-sandhā-vibhāgam । sukhākāri-dharmāñci-nīcaiḥ samīram ।। [bhujaṅgaprayātā] giriṃ līlayāspṛśya santaṃ hasantam । hariṃ hāri-rūpādibhiḥ prāg-avastham ।। [bhujaṅgaprayātā]
kadācin mudā sakhyur aṃse dadhānam । vrajāvāsi-loko yayau cātirītim ।। [bhujaṅgaprayātā] govardhanādris tatrāsīd ratna-citraṃ mahā-gṛham । harir yatra harid-ratna-stambhatārambhi-vibhramaḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh]
tad-upari parito' pi cchatra-tulyo girīndraḥ । vraja-sadana-janānāṃ pratyutābhūd vibhūtiḥ ।। [mālinī] [] tataś ca sahasā rohiṇī-sahitā vrajeśa-gṛhiṇī taṃ pārśvayor gṛhītavatī । tad idaṃ varṇibhir nirvarṇya varṇyate sma, yathā- pitrādy-ātmīya-vargaiḥ sa-pulakam abhito vīkṣito' tarkya-karmā ।
nyasta-kṣauṇī-bhṛd uccair jaya-jaya-ninadānvīḍitaḥ krīḍatīva ।। [sragdharā] govardhana-dharasyāgre vilāsān vyañjato balaḥ । kṛtsnān utsāhayaty eṣa nāṭye vā naṭa-nāyakaḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] tathā vajrīty evaṃvidha-vividha-gati-kleśa-hetur bahir yaḥ ।
marīciś citraśrīr ajitagiribhṛd ity āptaśarma vyakārīt ।। [śobhā] varyāṇāṃ svasti-pāṭhaḥ śruti-samaya-vidāṃ krīḍitaṃ bālakānām । sa śrī-govardhanādri-pravara-dhara-karaḥ kaṃ na toṣaṃ pupoṣa? ।।[sragdharā] kvacil līlālolā maghavati tu vakrā bata satī ।
kriyām anyāṃ tasya svam anu punar-uktām akuruta ।। [śikhariṇī] pibad iha paśu-jātaṃ sapta-rātrin-divāni । praṇayi-jana-gaṇānāṃ kiṃ bruve na bruve kim? ।। [mālinī] asya bhūdhara-dharasya pūryate ।
tan muhur bahu-rasair apūrayat ।। [rathoddhatā] tān kalpair api saptabhiḥ kathayitā śeṣo' pi nāśeṣataḥ । tūrṇaṃ varṇitavān kaviḥ svayam asau durbhūya dodūyate ।। [śārdūla] [] prathamaṃ tāvat prathamānena vātena vātena te pralayaṃ gatā iti sandihya, tadaiva tad-daivata-śatam eva tatra prabhūta-dūtatayā prasthāpitavān । tat tu tasmād atisatvaram āgatvaratayā tad abhīṣṭaṃ pratyācaṣṭa । tataś ca balārātir balāt pravartita-prasāreṇa jalāsāreṇa tad-vilāpanaṃ pratītya ca satyatā-pratipattaye jalada-devān eva tad-vārtāyāṃ vartayāmāsa । vartitāś ca te tad-vīkṣitena pathā pratyāgatya yathā-pūrvaṃ tat pratyāśā-padaṃ pratyākhyāya sthitavantaḥ । tataś ca paramam apūrvaṃ matvā, manasy atīva dhūrvaṇaṃ gatvā, ghanāghana-bṛṃhaṇaḥ sa ghanāghanaḥ sva-vāhanaṃ ghanāghanaṃ krodhād aṅkuśena maṅkṣu jaghāna । hatvā ca kiñcid agrato gatvā satvaram airāvatīya-vahnim ahni cāpahnuta-netra-vīryaṃ vikīrya dūtyāya tad-devatām avatārayāmāsa । sā ca tato nivṛtya pravṛtty-antaraṃ nivedayāmāsa-deva, paramāścarya-caryeyam avadhāryatām, yat khalu sa eva bali-bhojana-valita-balaḥ sann acalaḥ samyag utpatann ivāvalokyate ।
[] atha sarve yathājñāpayantīti vidrutya punaḥ saṅgatya saṃhatya pratyabhāṣanta-sarvadaiva sarva-daivata-mānya! śatamanyo! manyāmahe te sarve śata-parva-sagarbha-vidyud-vahninā pralīnatām eva nītāḥ, yad bahir na hi vilokyante । [] indra sa-harṣam uvāca-āyuṣmadbhir yuṣmābhir punar api nirūpyatām । [] atha tathā punaḥ saṅgatya gaty-antaraṃ prathayāmāsuḥ-divīśvara, nādyāpi te naśvaratāṃ prāptāḥ, pratyuta pātālatala iva giri-garta-tale praviśya tad diśantīvānanda-kolāhalaṃ kurvantaḥ pratīyante । acalaś ca svayaṃ balānuja-hasta-nyasta-prāya-grāva-nikāya-maya-kāyatayā pratīyate । [] indra uvāca-lakṣayāmi । mayā pūrvaṃ chinna-pakṣatir apy asau punaḥ kiṃ sa-pakṣaḥ sampannaḥ, yata eva garvavān sa parvataḥ sarvatas teṣām akṣayāya pakṣapātam ācacāra? bhavatu nāma, tam enaṃ punar nihrādi-hrādinī-vahni-prahāreṇa saṃhāre yojayāmi, yena tadīya-tale valamānatayā labdhāvalepās te' pi tūrṇam eva cūrṇatām āsādayanti iti ।
[] tathā ca, tad-vajreṇa biddhaṃ vidhāya praṇidhāna-dvārā tad anyathā praṇidhāya, manasi kopa-prakopam ādhāya, muhur api tad eva sandhāya, vyarthatā-kadarthita-puruṣārthaḥ punar nūtana-dūta-gaṇaṃ prahāpayann āha sma-are, nirūpyatāṃ tirobhūya, bhūyaḥ kiṃ tatra citram iva vartate, yenāśaner api pracāraḥ sva-vyavahārād vyabhicāraṃ sañcacāra । [] athāmī ca tathāgatya sva-pratyakṣaṃ pratyāyāmāsuḥ-sutrāman, na tatra kutracid api dvi-trāṇy api patrāṇi srastāni dṛśyante, na ca kācit pipīḍikāpi pīḍitā । tad evaṃ yady uparitanaṃ vṛttaṃ parito vṛttaṃ, tadā vilasita-raṅga-taraṅgāṇām antaraṅgānāṃ vārtā tu dūre vartatām । āṃ, kṛṣṇākāram anu viṣṇur eva tatrāvirbhaviṣṇutām āsasāda । kathaṃ vā sa ca parāt parājiṣṇutām āsīdatu, yaḥ khalv ahāryam api hāryatām āsādayāmāsa । [] atha tadānīm eva mūḍhaḥ, saṃjñayā śaṅkhacūḍaḥ, kaṃsa-sapakṣaḥ kaścid yakṣaḥ pratikṛṣṭam atitayātihṛṣṭaḥ saṅgamya praṇamya ca provāca-mahendradeva, drumila-dānava-nandana-mahīndra-sadanād bhavat-padāravindaṃ vindamānaḥ so' yam asmi । sa hi parama-hita-sahitatayā dundubhi-sandoha-nirghoṣaṃ pratidiśaṃ joṣayitvā bhavantaṃ prati prīti-pariṇāmaṃ praṇāmaṃ nirdideśa sandideśa ca । tad idaṃ bhavadbhir yad etad anuṣṭhitam, tena parama-tuṣṭim āpannā vayam । yataḥ kṣudratama-nirmita-garva-kirmīrita-mahad-atikramaḥ samastasya ca duḥsahaḥ sampadyate । balād utpatana-līla-pipīlikāvad amūdṛśāṃ tad-diṣṭataḥ prāpta-diṣṭāntatā ca dṛṣṭā । kiṃ ca, kiyad vābhīra-jātīnāṃ yajamānatayā bhavat-prayojanaṃ janitā? vayam eva hi nānā-yajñān anujñāpya bhavatsu santarpaṇam arpayiṣyāmaḥ ।
[] atha tad etad avadhārya sa deva-kula-nirdhāryaś camatkāram āsasāda, [] yatraivaṃ cintām āpa-aho, śakrāśana-vyasanatayā mama buddhir na sadā śuddhim avaruṇaddhi, yato mitrāmitratā vaiparītyaṃ parītya rīty-atikramam āpannavān asmi । tad etac ca, gotrabhid iti sva-nāma-sphurad-upaśruti-phalam iva mama pratibhāti । kiṃ ca, garviṇaḥ suṣṭhu me yuktāpy eṣābhibhava-bhāvanā । ātta-garvo' bhibhūtaḥ syād iti paryāyatā yataḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] prakāśas tu sva-dāsān uvāca-bhavatu, nivartantāṃ saṃvarta-vartanā megha-vārtāḥ । avarajanmāyam iti vrajarāja-tanūjaṃ prati titikṣā-bhāja eva vayaṃ śikṣā-mātra-pātratām āsāditavantaḥ, na tu katham apy anyathā-bhāva-bhāvana-vyathām iti ।
[] atha yakṣam apy ādidesa, nijaṃ rājānam idaṃ sandiśa-[] muhuḥ kopito' pi so' pi bhavāṃs tasmād bhayam iva bhāvayan vartata ity avadhārayata eva mamādhikaḥ krodhas tatra vardhate sma । yadi tad api tathyaṃ syāt tadā vayaṃ yāthātathyam eva prathayiṣyāmaḥ śatamanyoḥ sahasrākṣasya śatakoṭi-hastasya mamāpi kaḥ khalu khalatayānabhīpsitaṃ kurvīta? api ca- tvaṃ puṇya-janasevya-śrīr devānāṃ priyatāṃ gataḥ । so' py agre tvad-vidhānāṃ syād bhojānāṃ gopa-dārakaḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] tad etad anubhūya kupūyaḥ khalv asau dūyamāna-hṛdayatayā yakṣaḥ pratasthe, svena cānītaṃ sandeśaṃ pravāhe mūtritam ivātasthe ।
[] tad evam apadhvastaṃ-manyaḥ śatamanyuś ca śata-manyutayā vimāna-gatiṃ prati vimāna-gatim āsādya sadyaḥ sānuśayaṃ saṃśayānatayā śayānatayā ca nijāntar-nilayam ayāñcakre । śābdikāṣṭakam anu viśiṣṭatayā ralayor vyatyayam ivāvetya, nirayam eva ca taṃ manyate sma । tathā hi- varṣair dharṣayituṃ ca dharṣam agamad bāḍhaṃ viḍaujā hṛdi । sādhūtpāta-karatvam arjati viparyastā gatir yujyate ।। [śārdūlavikrīḍitam] diśaḥ sphuraṇam āgaman dharaṇir āpa vartma-prathām ।
idaṃ nija-nijāśraya-trayam anu svavṛttiṃ yayau ।। [pṛthvī] niryāta prātta-gṛhyā dara ca dara-matiṃ mā kurudhvaṃ tvaradhvam । bhūbhṛd-bhūtyā ca dhūtāḥ punar ahaha yayur garja-garvād vidhūtim ।। [sragdharā] [] atha tadāmreḍita-preritatayā vādita-bahula-kāhalādi-halahalāyamāna-kolāhalam ācarya haridāsa-varya-giri-hṛdayāyamāna-kuharāt tat-purata eva nirvrajan sa-go-samaja-vrajajana-samājaḥ sa-yaśaḥ-sneha-prasara-deha iva tasya virarāja ।
ārād apy antarantar giridhara-vadanaṃ draṣṭum āsan nivṛttaḥ । stabdhī-bhāvaṃ prapannaḥ, para-vaśa-daśayā tatra vaiyagryam āpa ।।[sragdharā] [] atha katham api nirgiri-vara-vivaraḥ sarvaḥ parasparam anuyānaṃ parīkṣya nirnimeṣatayā śrī-kṛṣṇa-niṣkramaṇaṃ pratīkṣya kṣaṇatas tad api nirīkṣya jīva iva jīvana-nibhaṃ tam āsīdan punar atīva mudam avāpa । yataḥ- khila-vyāpi-premā giri-dhṛtir api svāvana-kṛte ।
yadīyāḥ so' bhyāgān nijadṛśi gires tasya talataḥ ।। [śikhariṇī] yadvad utthāpitas tadvat kṛṣṇenādriḥ sa ropitaḥ । dṛṣṭaś ca sarva-lokena prakāras tu na lakṣitaḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] vivaśa-paśupa-lokā gotra-gartān milantam ।
dadhur anu nija-lābhaṃ vyutkramaṃ ca kramaṃ ca ।। [mālinī] bhavya-dravya-sabhājitaṃ viracayāmāsur jita-svarpatim । saṃvitte tad idaṃ sa eva ya idaṃ hṛdy anvabhūt karhy api ।। [śārdūla] yaśodā rohiṇī nando rāmaś ca balināṃ varaḥ ।
kṛṣṇam āliṅgya yuyujur āśiṣaḥ sneha-kātarāḥ ।।[] iti । [] tathā hi, ahaha, nava-navanīta-nīti-sukumārā kumāra-tanur iyam akharva-parvata-bhārataḥ kīdṛg abhavad bhavati bhaviṣyati ca iti sneha-maya-sandeha-rīti-bhītimantas te, tad etat kleśa-kulam asmad-vapur āveśaṃ sandeśatayā prayāsyati ity abhiprayanta iva, tam āśliṣyantas tatrāpy aviśvāsā iva, viśeṣād aśeṣāśiṣaḥ prayuñjānā, nija-vaṃśaṃ yaśasvatādi-yuktaṃ kurvāṇā iva, te tat-tan-nāmnā samāmnātāś ciraṃ bāṣpa-niṣpatti-bhitta-netra-vṛttayaḥ saṃvṛttāḥ । [] tatra yadyapi yaugapadyatas tūrṇam eva caturṇāṃ milanaṃ samapadyata, tathāpi prema-tāratamyam anukramya kṛṣṇāvadhāna-kramaḥ kramate sma yasmāt tasmād eva tathā śrī-śuka-devaḥ pracakrame yaśodety-ādinā । [] yatra jñāna-kriyā-śaktibhyāṃ balaṃ valamānasyāpi baladevasya tādṛśī sneha-kātaratā niratā, tatra kimutāparasya । sa khalv apara eveti । tatra ca-
dvāv apy aṅgakulaṃ nibhālya paritaḥ papracchatuḥ śantamam । pretyekānvitam eva sevanam adhuḥ prāṇā hi sarvasya saḥ ।। [śārdūla] [] atrāparāpi kautuka-paramparāvadhāryatām । [] gate ca kaṃsa-pakṣe yakṣe yadā sa khalu vṛddhaśravā vṛddhaśravastvam evātmānaṃ pratimanyate sma, tadā sāvahittham idam utthāpitavān-bho madīya-gaṇāḥ, samavadhīyatām । sa khalu dānavārir vārita-mad-udyamatayā vipakṣavad ācarann api vairi-śamanatayā mayā sahāyatayā niścitas tat-parīkṣārtham eva ca tathā vibhīṣita ity abhinandanīya eva bhavadbhiḥ iti । divi deva-gaṇāḥ sādhyāḥ siddha-gandharva-cāraṇāḥ ।
tuṣṭuvur mumucus tuṣṭāḥ puṣpa-varṣāṇi sarvataḥ ।। śaṅkha-dundubhayo nedur divi devādi-vāditāḥ । jagur gandharva-patayo yeṣāṃ tumburur āditaḥ ।। [] kṛta-stavatayā calan-mudita-gopa-vṛndair vṛtaḥ । sphurat-parama-sampadaṃ vrajam agād vrajeśātmajaḥ ।। [pṛthvī]
kṣatāntimārtha-pracitā yathā te । kiñcic ca nājñāsiṣur artha-nāśam ।। [upajāti ] [] giri-gartān niṣkramaṇe yathoktaṃ śrī-bādarāyaṇinā gopyaś ca sa-sneham apūjayan mudā dadhy-akṣatādibhiḥ [] iti । śailam apy adhṛtaḥ yaḥ svakān avan ।
uddhūtaṃ vyadhita dūra-deśataḥ ।। [indravajrā] dhṛtvā girim asau naikadhuratām āgataḥ param । bhavatāṃ jagatāṃ cāgād api sarva-dhurīṇatām ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] tad evaṃ kathā-prathana-pūrvakaṃ pūrvavan nija-nija-prayojanāya kṛta-vrajanāyāṃ janatāyām anukṛṣṇaṃ raveḥ samastam astaṃ yāvat kṛta-vihārau sūta-kumārau punar api rajanī-sabhāyāṃ sabhājitau nanditājitau babhūvatuḥ ।
vistāram āyāti tathā bakīripoḥ । prathīyasī kā bata kā tanīyasī? ।। [upajāti ] [] tām apy asmākaṃ grantha-lāghavāya saṅkocayatāṃ kaviṣu lāghavam eva paryavasyati । tathāpy akuṇṭha-buddhyā svayam eva sā bahudhā budhyatām । ity uktvā bhrātaram āha sma, ārya kathakācārya bhūyaḥ śrūyatām- paraṃ girer eva satraṃ hariṇā na prakāśitam ।
kintu śrī-rādhikādīnām ānanendu-rucer api ।। yadā tu makha-sambhāraḥ kṛṣṇena vipulīkṛtaḥ । tadālaṅkāra-sambhāras tābhir apy urarīkṛtaḥ ।। yadā dīpālir ajvāli śikharaṃ śikharaṃ prati । sa cāmūś ca mithas tarhi vyadṛśyantāvṛta-sthalāt ।। yadā pravartitas tasmin bakahantrā girer mahaḥ । prāvarti ca tadā tābhis tad-didṛkṣā-mahā-mahaḥ ।। yadā samuditā jātā mahilā bhūmi-bhṛn makhe ।
tadā tā muditā jātā hari-darśana-niściteḥ ।। kṛṣṇe saṃlāpam ācerur yadā vividha-subhruvaḥ । tadārha-bodha-sadṛśaṃ dṛśaṃ tāś ca nyayūyujan ।। yadādrir janatā-dṛṣṭiṃ kṛṣṭavān prakaṭī-bhavan । āśādhāma yayuḥ svairaṃ tadāsām akṣi-pakṣiṇaḥ ।। yadā go-pūjanaṃ kartum ārabdhaṃ sarvakais tadā । tābhiḥ pratisva-dhenv-arcā-praśnāspadam akāri saḥ ।। yadā gopāla-pūjāyā maho vyaktam abhūd bahiḥ ।
tadā mano-mahas tāsāṃ vaktre vaktre vyalokyata ।। gopa-pṛṣṭhaṃ yadā dṛṣṭaṃ kanyāpāṇyaṅkitaṃ puru । tadāsāṃ pāṇayaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ spraṣṭum utkaṇṭhitāṃ gatāḥ ।। homa-kāle yadā kṛṣṇaḥ prāviśad brahma-saṃsadi । hutaṃ bata tadā tābhir mānasaṃ virahānale ।। gireḥ parikrame yarhi vyavadhānaṃ yayau hariḥ । tadā tāṃ vyavadhām eva girīyanti sma tat-priyāḥ ।। yaṣṭiṃ yarhy utkṣipan gṛhṇan kṛṣṇaś cakrāma tarhi tām ।
dṛṣṭvā dūrād añjanāsrair bhānujā bhānujāyate ।। yadā yadā mitho rūpaṃ draṣṭum āsīd asambhavaḥ । gavānudrava-lakṣyeṇa sa tāsāṃ madhyam adravat ।। dhenv-anudravaṇa-vyājāt spṛśan vavrāja yāṃ hariḥ । cillī-vallī-tāḍyamānas tayā sa stambham īyivān ।। yadā rādhām anu spṛṣṭiṃ dṛṣṭir asya gatā tadā । ayaṃ sarvaṃ visasmāra kintu sasmāra tan-mukham ।। yadā rātrāv abhūd vāsaḥ sarveṣām eka-dhāmani ।
tac-chabda-mātra-tāt-paryāḥ śrutitāṃ tarhi tāḥ yayuḥ ।। kṛṣṇāyās tu yadā kṛṣṇaś cikrīḍa srotasi svayam । tadāmodiny amūs tasminn akrīḍann atidūrataḥ ।। bhaginīnāṃ gṛhe yarhi bhoktum abhyāyayau hariḥ । sakhya-lakṣyāt tadā tāsāṃ sarvās tatrāpy amūr gatāḥ ।। yathā-pūrvaṃ yadā sarve pratisvaṃ vāsam avrajan । tadā kārā-gṛhe hanta menire tāḥ punar gatim ।। yadā saṃvarta-meghās te prāvartanta tadā tu tāḥ ।
akāmayanta kṛṣṇāya sva-svaccha-trāyamāṇatām ।। yadā suhṛdbhiś chatrādyair lālitaṃ tam alokayan । svāṅga-bhetrīm amūr vṛṣṭiṃ tadā saudhīm amaṃsata ।। vichinna-prakharāsāra-cchatre tatreha dīvyati । kṛṣṇe svairaṃ gatā dṛṣṭiṃ menire vṛṣṭim āmṛtīm ।। abhi kṛṣṇaṃ yadā sarvaḥ śaila-garte' nvavartata । gṛha-prāpta-nidhīnāṃ vā tadā tāsāṃ sthitir matā ।। [anuṣṭubh]
harer mukha-sudhā-rasaṃ rasanayā dṛg-ākārayā । kutaḥ sukṛtam udgataṃ na iti vismṛtīr avrajan ।। [pṛthvī] svacche netra-jale tad-īkṣaṇa-bhave koṣṇatvam itthaṃ gatā । kāntasyāniśa-darśitasya ca cirād adriḥ kare dṛśyate ।। [śārdūlavikrīḍitam]
nijārthita-vinākṛtām api diśaṃ sa ninye muhuḥ । tadā phala-mayaṃ mama śramatamaḥ prasajjed iti ।। [pṛthvī] samastam abhitarkyate tad iha citta-dhairyaṃ bhaja । vapuś ca tava rakṣitety akṛta bhāvam eṣā tadā ।। [pṛthvī]
murāres taṃ prāṇa-pratimam apahāyāpi nirayuḥ । tad āsāṃ viśliṣṭer bharam asahamāno niragamat ।। [śikhariṇī] kiṃ sa vā sva-hṛdayād iti sphuṭam । tarhi yarhi niragād asau priyaḥ ।। [rathoddhatā]
bhūri-bhūmi-valayeṣu mṛgākṣyaḥ । tat kim apy akathayan nija-hārdam ।। [svāgatā] rādhe parito yāsīd govardhana-dhāriṇas tadā karuṇā । sāsrān nayana-prāntāt prāntāt tvayy eva sā suviśrāntā ।। [anuṣṭubh]
[] tad etad api kathana-śeṣaṃ samāpya pūrvavad eva sūta-sutayor gatayoḥ sarve' pi yathāsvaṃ prasthitāḥ । ।। [] tad evaṃ tādṛk-sampadi pratipadi govardhana-samardhanaṃ siddham । tṛtīyām ārabhya navamy-avadhikaṃ ramyaṃ tad-dhāraṇam addhāvadhāryatām । [] atha tādṛśa-daśā-ramyāyāṃ daśamyāṃ śrī-vraja-rāja-samājam anu nimantraṇayā prāmāṇi-kamāṇikya-vraja-janāḥ sukha-yojanaṃ bhojanaṃ saṃyujya mukha-vāsanaṃ mukha-vāsam upajyujya vārtāṃ vartayāmāsuḥ । [] yatra kṣitidhara-dhāraṇa-nidhyānān nirdhārayantaḥ pūtanāvadhādikam etad avadhikam asambhāvitaṃ sambhāvitaṃ cāviśeṣatayā tat-karma-viśeṣatayā gaṇayāmāsuḥ ।
vāvahiḥ parvataṃ bālaḥ sāsahir na tu cācaliḥ । bahir eva yathā vṛṣṭiḥ pāpatir na tad-antare ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] tad evaṃ parama-prabhāvatā tāvad vismaya-jananī jananītim atikrāmati । tasyām api satyāmatyāsakti-maya-sneha-caya-svabhāvatā mādṛśām anyādṛśām api tasmin niścitā vismitim ātanoti । [] tasya ca mādṛkṣu visadṛkṣu ca yāsau lakṣyate, sā tu parama-vilakṣaṇatayātīva vailakṣyaṃ lakṣayati । kiṃ ca- sarveṣāṃ nas tadīye sa katham atha kathaṃ śakyate nāpi moktuṃ ।
smāraṃ smāraṃ tad etat na katham api manāg uktiyuktī vrajāmaḥ ।। [sragdharā] [] tad evaṃ pravaṇatayā śravaṇataḥ śrīmān nandaḥ prajātānandaḥ praṇaya-mayatayā sammata-samayatayā ca garga-siddhānta-vargam evānugadya niravadya-sauhṛdyatas teṣām amandehodbhava-sandehodyamaṃ saṃyamanam anaiṣīt, śrūyatāṃ me vaco gopo vyetu śaṅkā ca vo' rbhake [] ity ādinā । ante coktavān- prāsthita gargas tad-avadhi jānāmi । valayati nārāyaṇī yayā śaktyā ।। [gīti]
[] tad evaṃ śrīman-nanda-rāja-vākyatas tad-avakalanānanda-bhājas taṃ yadā samasta-janāḥ samasta-janānandana-tan-nandana-vārtayā nandayantaḥ santi sma, tadā nija-vṛndair vṛndārakaiś ca vandyamānatayā nandyamānatayā nandyamānatayā ca vṛndāvana-candraḥ sahasā saha-rāmaḥ samājagāma । [] samājaś cāyaṃ samam eva taṃ pariveṣa iva paritaś chādayāmāsa, cakora-vāra iva tat-kāntim āsvādayāmāsa, vārāṃ nidhir iva cātmānam ullolatayā sampādayāmāsa । [] tad evaṃ sthite sarvasminn api svasthatayā cāvasthite kṣaṇa-katipaye ca prasthite sarva eva te sāmājikāḥ pratisvam amanendirād ātma-mandirād ānīta-prīta-sitāsita-praśasta-vastra-saṅkaraṃ sad-alaṅkaraṇādikaṃ taṃ ca tad-bhrātaraṃ tat-pitaraṃ ca pṛthak pṛthag alaṅkāraṃ svīkārayāñcakruḥ । [] yathaivaṃ bahir ebhir ācaritaṃ, tathāntaḥ-pure sa-rāma-mātṛkāṃ giridharasya mātaram abhi caiṣāṃ mahilābhir viracitam iti nirviśeṣam eva tad ubhayatra parvāsīt ।
[] atha sura-pure sureśasya vṛttam anuvṛtyatām । [] ito gatvā dainyaṃ matvā skhalad-ojā viḍaujāḥ kṣayaṃ gacchann apy asau kṣayam ṛcchann iva sthitavān na tu śacīm acīkamata, na ca nirjara-sadasi nirjagāma । [] tad evaṃ varṇyamānam avakarṇya vācaspatir vāstoṣpatim anurahasaṃ bhartsayāmāsa, yataḥ sa khalu vibudhānām api vibudhaḥ । [] bhartsanaṃ, yathā- yasmād abhajasi viṣṇuṃ jiṣṇo tasmād anedhitāse tvam । na vinā candraṃ vindati jīvana-vṛttiṃ vanaspatiḥ ko' pi ।। [gīti]
[] athavā sahasradṛśam apy aho bhavādṛśam abhibhūya bhṛśī-bhavantī tādṛśī madāndhatā nāsadṛśī, yataḥ sureśo' si । kintv amṛtapatā tava kathaṃ mrtapatā jātā? yatas tyakta-prāṇa-prāyaṇa-kāya-prāyataḥ pramādaḥ so' yam āpatitaḥ । apasnāta iva snāto' py alam aspṛśya eva saḥ । mṛtakaṃ vapur āsajjan yaḥ sadbhyo bhaya-dāyakaḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] kiṃ ca-vṛṣāhvaya, tava cedam atyavicārata eva । tathā hi-
yad-ālambāj janaḥ prāṇaṃ yasmād rakṣitum icchati । vaiparītyaṃ tayoḥ kurvann anunmatto na kathyate ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] indra uvāca-avicāritam evācaritam idaṃ mayā, bhavadbhiś ca sāmprataṃ sāmpratam upadiśyatām । [] vācaspatir uvāca-śatamanyo, tādṛśa-visadṛśatāyāṃ śatadhṛtir eva dhṛtim āsādayitā, tasmāt tad-anusaraṇam eva śaraṇam ।
[] tad evaṃ jambhabhedī sakhedī-bhavann avadhāya dhātāram eva gatvā saṅkocam amatvā svāparādham avadhārayāmāsa । [] sa tūvāca-hanta, vibudhādhipenāpy abudhena bhavatā bhavatā duḥsādha-rādhaḥ so' yaṃ mahān evāparādhaḥ kṛtaḥ, yaṃ khalu sādhavaḥ sakṛd apy avadhārayantas tvām avadhīrayantaḥ sāvadhānāḥ śrotram apidadhate । tathāpi sṛṣṭi-vidhitsā-durvidhinā vidhinā mayā tad idam upadiśyate । pūrvaṃ tan-mahima-jijñāsayā dhārṣṭyam anuṣṭhitam astīti tan-mātra-kilbiṣa-viṣama-viṣama-viṣaha-mānena mayā durmāṇa-mayāgādha-bhavad-aparādha-kṣamāpaṇāya kṣamatā na labhyate । gavāṃ kaṇḍūyanaṃ kuryād go-grāsaṃ go-pradakṣiṇām । nityaṃ goṣu prasannāsu gopālo' pi prasīdati ।।
iti gautamādi-sammatyā gojātiṣu prīti-rīti-parītasya tasya kṣamāpaṇāya kātaras tvaṃ taj-jāti-mātaraṃ surabhīm eva bhajasva, na ced asurataḥ surabhī-saṅgatir bhaviṣyati । [] atha sunāsīras tv asurabhītaḥ surabhī-lokam āsādya sadyas tad avadya-carita-pracārād vimanasam api tāṃ mātuḥ svasāraṃ muhuḥ prasādya vedhasaḥ savidham evānināya । [] tataś ca vidhātedam abhidadhe-ayi, surabhi, surapati-bhī-sāntvanārtham asurāntakasyāntikaṃ gaccha । gatvā ca tvam asya nūnam evam eva labdha-duścyavana-nāmnaḥ parikilbiṣa-kīrtana-bhiyā kila kavi-pariṣad-upekṣaṇīya-tan-nāma-dheyasya kṛṣṇataś cyavanaṃ vicyāvaya । tac ca sva-sampad-upakaṇṭha-kuṇṭhī-kṛtāpara-vaikuṇṭha-loka-goloka-mahendratā-martya-loke' py asya vyaktībhavatād iti tad-abhiṣeka-sevātirekataḥ sambhāvitā iti । [] atha hari-vāsara-divase surabhiḥ sura-rājam anu vṛndāvana-bhūpari-bhuvar-loka-bhāgam āgamya tad-avasaraṃ pratīkṣāmāsa । tatra ca dūrataḥ sura-patiṃ surabhir abhihitavatī-
nāyaṃ navyas tasya bhāgaḥ sa kṛṣṇaḥ । naitan mandaṃ garjitaṃ narmavārtā ।। [śālinī] [] paśya paśya, samyag utpatiṣṇuḥ pataga-jiṣṇur viṣṇu-vāhanaḥ so' yam asmad apy upari-bhāgam ārūḍhaḥ san vidyud-gūḍha-vārida-vāra iva yasya cchāyām icchan kila yatra cchāyāṃ prasārayati । [] so' yaṃ tu- vāmoru-sthita-kañja-cāru-caraṇe savyaṃ karaṃ dakṣiṇe ।
smereṇākṣi-taṭena sandadhad aho manye kṛpāṃ varṣati ।। [śārdūla] [] atra cāyam asman-milanam aṅgīkurvann eva saṅginaḥ prasaṅgāntarāya prasthāpitavān । baladevaś ca nādya vanam āgatavān iti cāsthīyate । tasmād atisvacchatara-cetasam amuṃ bhavāṃs tāvan nibhṛtatayā nibhṛtam avyagratayā cābhyagraṃ gatvā daṇḍavan natvā prasādayitum arhati । yataḥ, svayam aparādhyati kurute prabhum abhi tan-mārjane sahāyaṃ yaḥ । tasyedaṃ para-śakter darśanam atha naiva dainyasya ।। [āryā]
yasmin svayam aparādhī namati rahas taṃ sahāya-nirviṇṇaḥ । kṛpayati sā jana-mātraṃ dainyāvasthā mahājanaṃ kim uta? ।। [gīti] [] tataś ca paścād eva viśeṣa-nivedanāyām aham āyāsyāmi । [] atha pāka-śāsanas tad-anuśāsanam urarīkṛtya pracchannatayā muralī-dhara-samīpam āgatya pratyagraṃ caraṇa-khara-daṇḍayor daṇḍavat papāta ।
agryām amuṣya mukuṭe maṇitām avāpuḥ । mādhvīka-vidrava-vidhau vidhutām agacchan ।। [vasantatilakā] [] atha krandati saṅkrandane paṅkaja-locanaḥ saṅkocitaḥ kirīṭāgram agra-hastena sāgraham udastam ācarann uvāca-[] bhagavann, evam ayuktaṃ mā kārṣīr, ārṣīṇāṃ vāṇīnāṃ tvam eka evātirekataḥ parāyaṇam asi । [] vajrapāṇis tu mūrdhni prasajjitāñjali-pāṇitayā salajjaṃ svayaṃ svavajra-hata iva maunam evāsasajja । yataḥ-
parasya kāyaṃ badhnāti tejasā vacasā manaḥ । śaktaḥ śaktaś ca so' yaṃ yas tasya bhaktaḥ kathaṃ na kaḥ? ।। [anuṣṭubh] anyatra candrati hariḥ śakre tarhi sma sūryati । śakro' pi sūryaty anyasmin khadyotati harau sma saḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh]
yadā maunaṃ sasajjāsau tadā mūka ivābhavat । yadā tu stotum ārabdhas tadāgād vāvadūkatām ।। [anuṣṭubh] yathāmūṃ stutavān indras tathā vaktuṃ na śakyate । śrī-vrajendra yataḥ so' yaṃ tvattaḥ saṅkucati sphuṭam ।। [anuṣṭubh]
mayedaṃ bhagavan goṣṭha-nāśāyāsāra-vāyubhiḥ । ceṣṭitaṃ vihate yajñe māninā tīvra-manyunā ।।[] iti । mayā te' kāri maghavan makha-bhaṅgo' nugṛhṇatā । [] yan mat-pitrādi-sac-chreṣṭhān nātikrāmer mama smaran ।। [anuṣṭubh]
suraś ced viṣayābhoga-garvād roceta vāsava । tadā vipraś ca śobheta śauṣkalaṃ-manyatā-madāt ।। [anuṣṭubh] aham unmūlayiṣyāmi śakra tvad-vairi-pakṣagān । kathaṃ man manyase bhītiṃ nītim eva pravartaya ।। [anuṣṭubh]
[] atha dūrataḥ surabhir abhītam iva tam abhīkṣya, huṅkārataḥ sva-santāna-santānam ākārya, kārya-viduṣī sa-tṛṣṇa-nayanā kṛṣṇam abhijagāma । [] kṛṣṇaś ca svajāti-rītikāvasthitita evāvanamantīm iva tām imāṃ sahasā sahasām asasambhramam añjali-sañjita-karaḥ sañjagāda-mātā kathaṃ samāyātā? ete mad-anvayā dhanyā gotvaṃ tvāṃ sevituṃ gatāḥ । ahaṃ tu nedṛk-puṇyā yad gocaratvaṃ ca nāgatā ।। [anuṣṭubh] daitya-ghātī bhavān nityaṃ sarva-lokaika-pālakaḥ ।
vayaṃ ca loka-madhye smas tvan-nāthāḥ svata eva tat ।। [anuṣṭubh] go-sūktaṃ bhāṣate gāvaḥ padaṃ sarva-suparvaṇām । tad brahmādau suparvatvam avan vinda gavendratām ।। [anuṣṭubh] tavedaṃ kiyad aiśvaryaṃ yad brahmāvadhi-pālanaṃ ।
vaikuṇṭha-kuṇṭhatā-kāri yasya goloka-vaibhavam ।। [anuṣṭubh] sarvasya pālakāt kvāpi khaṇḍa-pālanam iṣyate । jagat-prakāśakād bhānor nija-dhāma-prakāśavat ।। [anuṣṭubh] nāsmākaṃ kevalam idaṃ mataṃ kintu vidher api ।
yad bhaved asya cendrasya durbuddheḥ śuddhi-bhāvanam ।। [anuṣṭubh] tvat-kṛpāyāḥ paraṃ sthānaṃ vayam ity eṣa vāsavaḥ । āśiśriye yad asmāṃs tad dvāra-mātrāya kalpate ।। [anuṣṭubh] yasmān mṛgyati tām eva mad-vidhād bhavataḥ kṛpām ।
kūpād iva rasāntaḥ-sthāṃ tarṣī ghana-rasa-sthitim ।। [anuṣṭubh] tad eva deva paśyendraḥ paśyaṃs tava pada-dvayam । sūcayaty abhiṣekaṃ te netra-dhārā-sahasrataḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] atha tatra sacita-saṅkocanena vilocanena gocaritānumateḥ śrī-gokula-pateḥ prasādam āsādayantī surarṣi-sura-mātṛ-surapati-suratatibhir upasura-prabhṛtibhiś ca sākaṃ surabhī sarabhasam asura-mardanaṃ puraskartuṃ puraḥ-saratām avāpa ।
[] te hi druhiṇena tāv anu samanujñātā drutam eva vidrutya nihnutya ca rājīva-locanaṃ rājīyantaḥ paritaḥ sthitā babhūvuḥ, yatra rudra-druhiṇāv api teṣām agresaratām avāpatuḥ । [] tataś ca surabhir abhihitavatī-śrīmad-vrajendra-kula-candra! bhavad-bhavadīya-svīya-caraṇānām anucaraṇatas tāvad atratyāni tīrthāni sārthakāny eva jātāni । dhenavaś ca yuṣmad-vihita-dugdha-dhayanād dhanyatām adhuḥ । [] tataś ca svarga-sthita-tīrtha-varasya gaṅgā-nirjharasya tathātmīyasyāpy ūdho-bharasya tvad-ārādhanayā vyarthatāvadhāya payaḥ samāhartuṃ bhavantaṃ vidhim arthayāmahe । athavā, yathādiśyate tathāvaśyaṃ prathayāmaḥ । [] kṛṣṇaḥ sa-smitam uvāca-yatheṣṭham anuṣṭhīyatām । [] athābhravāhana-bhrū-bhramaṇataḥ sa-sambhramam abhra-mātaṅgaḥ svaḥ-saṅgata-gaṅgātaḥ samuddaṇḍita-śuṇḍā-daṇḍenāmbhaḥ-sambhṛtān nidhi-kumbhān nirvilambam eva muhur api lambhayāmāsa । surabhir api surabhi-payasā sura-pati-sarasīm upagiriṃ vibharāñcakāra । tataś ca-
harṣāndolātikolāhala-jaya-ninadair brahma-rudrādikānām । kṛṣṇaṃ yenaiva sarve' py ahaha sukha-sudhāsikta-rūpā babhūvuḥ ।। [sragdharā] aditir mātṛ-kṛtyāni svasṛ-kṛtyāni pārvatī । garutmān bhṛtya-kṛtyāni cāhṛtyātra mudaṃ yayau ।। [anuṣṭubh]
maṅgalya-dhvāna-dhārā dig-anuga-kariṇāṃ prāviśat karṇa-gartam । śāte jāte' pi kaṃsaḥ saraṭa-paṭala-rāṭ-ceṣṭayā veṣṭyate sma ।। [sragdharā] śrī-goloka-padaṃ praśastim ayate lakṣmī-parārdhāspadam । tena tvaṃ jagad aṅga tadvad avatād ity ucire te samam ।। [śārdūla]
ākāśa-kusumaiḥ sārdham ākāśa-vacanaṃ tadā । govinda iti yad vittaṃ tataḥ kim iva sādbhutam? ।। [anuṣṭubh] brahmā līlābjam īśaḥ svaracita-muralīṃ mādhavāya vyatānīt । pūrvaṃ cāpūrvam āsīd abhavad atha tad-aṅgāvṛtījyāsu pūjyam ।। [sragdharā]
bhrāmyad-vālavya-jana-yugalaṃ prasphurad-divya-veśam । citrāṇīva kṣaṇa-katipayaṃ tatra mitrāṇi tasthuḥ ।। [mandākrāntā] [] tataś ca kṛpayā snapita-nayanāravindena govindena kṛtam ānandanam anu phullatayā pūrvataḥ puruṣu mahendrādi-deva-guruṣu chatrādikaṃ taruṣu sandhāya, nija-hita-nibandhāya tat-pada-dvandvam eva vandaṃ vandam amanda-bāṣpa-nisyandaṃ nijām avajñāspadatāṃ vijñāpya tam anujñāpya dūraṃ vindamāneṣu labdha-vigata-nindamāneṣu vṛndārakeṣu, sakhi-sandohaḥ śandoham anuvindan mandaṃ mandam āsasāda । āsādya ca- chatrādyaṃ ca cacāya mitrapaṭalī papraccha bhūyaś ca tam ।
kintu prītibharaṃ mithaḥ pravalayaṃ hāsas tad āvardhata ।। [śārdūla] vibhuḥ parasparam api tām abhūṣayat । paricchedaiḥ svayam api taṃ siṣevire ।। [rucirā] vargais tad-guṇa-rūpa-śīla-tulitaiḥ sva-pratta-tat-tac-chriyā ।
sva-premārjita-karma-sampadam amaṃstānyan na mānyaṃ tataḥ ।। [śārdūla] pṛthvīṃ dugdha-bhṛtāṃ vyadhur bahu-vidhān nadyo rasān susruvuḥ । jīvāḥ prāpur aho mahaty apacitiḥ puṣyaty akartṝn api ।। [śārdūlavikrīḍita] cittaṃ kampam iyarti ced giri kathaṃ cittena tad vyajyatām ।
āyāti svayam eva ced giri kathaṃ cittena sā vyajyatām? ।। [śārdūla] saṃsevyamāna-savidhaḥ sakhibhiḥ pragītaḥ । śrī-pṛkta-kāntir ajitaḥ sadanaṃ sasāda ।। [vasantatilakā] dyujani-vibhūṣaṇa-bhūṣaṇāṅgam etam ।
ajani ca sāttvika-rājirāji-mūrtiḥ ।। [puṣpitāgrā] [] yat tu niśamya ramyacetā rāmaḥ sānukrośaṃ krośamātram upavrajya nijāvarajavijayaṃ paśyan sukha-vaśyamanās tam āliṅgya mūrdhānam āśiṅghya kṣaṇa-katipayam upaviśya, vacana-cāturībhis tat-prasaṅgaṃ saṅgatavān । tataś ca nijānujena pūrvam eva svakṛte nirdiśya rakṣitair divyeṣv api divyatā-lakṣitair analpair ākalpaiḥ so' yam agrajaḥ sva-kareṇa virājayāmāsa । tataś ca svānujaṃ guru-janānām agratas tādṛśatayā prayātuṃ saṅkocam arocayan so' yam agrajaḥ śanaiḥ sanair anaiṣīt । [] atha tasmin dine tu go-sandoha-doha-nibandhanaṃ tad-anubandhi-janān sandhāya svayaṃ tu tat-tad-udantānusandhānāya dhenu-sannidhāna eva sānandaṃ nanda-rājaḥ sannidhāya, vandamānaṃ sa-rāma-sakhi-vṛndaṃ govindaṃ purastād vidhāya samam eva bandhubhiḥ samam āsanam āsajjann āsāmāsa । [] tatra cānantaram ācaritāgatibhiḥ samyag urīkṛta-śrī-rāmānujānumatibhiḥ sūnṛta-vādibhiḥ śrīdāmādibhiḥ sa-samājāya vraja-rājāya divyac-chatrādy-arcāmatrādiṣu samarpiteṣu santarpiteṣu ca sarveṣu tad apracchannam eva sa papraccha-kathyatāṃ tathyaṃ kim idaṃ vṛttaṃ vṛttam? iti ।
[] śrīdāmā prāha-vayam api go-saṅkalanāya kalita-bhūri-dūratayā ciraṃ viramya sthitā na samyag avagamyaṃ tad ācarāma, kintu sāmagrīyam eva nija-samyag-rītim āvedayati iti । [] tato namratāṃ vindati śrī-govinde parasparam avadhāya sādhu, śrīdāman, sādhv idam uktam ity abhidhāya sarva evānarvācīna-gopāś citra-pratikṛtaya iva dvitra-kṣaṇaṃ nirnimeṣatām avāpuḥ । naṃsīt ko' pi karī sitaḥ svar-udakāny āhṛtya śaśvad dadau । te cānye ca mahāmahena siṣicur gopeśa putraṃ tava ।। [śārdūlavikrīḍita]
saṃsajya govindatayā sutaṃ tava । taṃ yauvarājyena javād virājaya ।। [upajāti ] [] atha tad etad amṛta-varṣa-dharṣitā vraja-varṣīyāṃsaḥ parasparaṃ vicārya kārya-māṇa-maṅgalya-tauryatrika-vādanāpaurvāparyataḥ svasti-vācanādikam ācārya-dvārā samācārya, pratisvam api vividha-vidhāna-dāna-pūrvakaṃ parva pūrayitvā pūra-rājatayā taṃ sabhājayāmāsuḥ । pratyekaṃ maṇi-dīpa-santati-karā maṅgala-kolāhalāḥ ।
snehaṃ mūrtam ivātiyatna-valitā govindam āninyire ।। [śārdūlavikrīḍita] īdṛśas te vrajādhīśa sutaḥ sūta-mukhotsavaḥ । yo gavendratayā gāṃ ca gāṃ ca gāṃ ca sukhākarot ।। [anuṣṭubh] subhagambhaviṣṇu jātaṃ jagad api kṛṣṇābhiṣekataḥ paścāt ।
andhambhāvukam āsīd bhāvuka-śūnyaṃ kulaṃ tu danujānām ।। [gīti] [] tad evaṃ divā-kathāyāṃ vṛttāyāṃ naktam api sā pūrvavad vṛttā । yathā madhukaṇṭha uvāca- bhaved analpaṃ kutrāpi svalpaṃ kutrāpi poṣakam । yathānna-vyañjanaṃ loke yathā rasa-rasāyanam ।। [anuṣṭubh]
[] tasmāt saṅkṣiptam apy etad vistaravad eva mantavyam । [] tathā hi-tasmin mahasi nīrandhraṃ purandhrībhiḥ samam āsām api samāganaṃ vṛttaṃ, yatropakaṇṭha-gatānām apy amūṣāṃ vastrāvaguṇṭhitāni netrāṇy atīvotkaṇṭhitāni jātāni । dhanyā yayā tu karapīḍanam asya gantā? । astaṃ nināya bata nas tam amūṃ dhig astu ।। [vasantatilakā] bhṛd-utkaṇṭhākaṇṭhāgata-tulita-jīvā bata vayam ।
tathāpy eṣā hā dhik kalita-hari-saṅgā na tu vayam ।। [śikhariṇī] māle kaṭaṃ prakaṭam eva sadā dadhāsi । saṅkoca-leśam ayate tvam ato' si dhanyā ।। [vasantatilakā] ardhaṃ kācid vraja-jana-gatā kācid asyās tribhāgam ।
sarvāsāṃ yan manasi caklpe hanta tāpāya tadvat ।। [mandākrāntā] [] atha tasyām eva niśāyāṃ candraśālikāyāṃ kṛta-śayanena kañja-nayanena tāsām aparāhnetanāpāṅga-sāṅga-śara-nikara-saṅga-labdha-bhaṅge hṛdi samutthita-vyathatayā jāta-niśītha-jāgaratāyām aviratāyāṃ tāsu nijānirvṛtiṃ vivṛtīkartuṃ tām iva ca tartuṃ purahara-kṛta-vitara-nava-muralīkalaḥ khuralībhiḥ kalayāmāse । tadā kedāra-rāgas tu prāpa kedāratāṃ niśi । gopībhir vāsanā-bījam uptaṃ yatrāṅkurāyitam ।। [anuṣṭubh]
so' yaṃ vaiṇava-gānataḥ pratipadaṃ prāyaḥ parāmṛśyate । matvā svaṃ prati tat pratisvam api tāḥ sarvā vimūrcchāṃ yayuḥ ।। [śārdūla] āsv adhād yad avidus tad amūś ca । svaṃ ca samprati viveda na rādhā ।। [svāgatā]
so' yaṃ te ramaṇo rādhe labdhaḥ kṛcchreṇa yas tvayā । tvad-vinā-bhāvataḥ saukhyaṃ yaś ca kutrāpi nāptavān ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] tad evaṃ saṅkṣepenāpi kathite prathite muhūrta-dvayaṃ muhūrtavad eva tāś ca te ca tuṣṇīmbhāvam āseduḥ, punaś ca yathāyatham āvāsaṃ samāseduḥ । ।।
[] atha prabhāta-kathāyāṃ snigdhakaṇṭha uvāca-tad evam ekādaśī-kathā kathitā । tāṃ ca tithim aśithilitayā prathita-manorathāṃ pratītya nityavad eva vraja-devaḥ samyag ullāsam upovāsa । [] kintu pāraṇa-kāraṇam avaśīrṇam eva dvādaśīm avaśiṣṭām avadhāya bahv-avaśiṣṭāyām api rajanyāṃ viśiṣṭa-vidhi-balataḥ snānādi-kalanāya kalindīṃ praviṣṭavān । praviśya ca yathā-yatham atrasnuḥ sasnau । snātvā cāntar eva vāriṇaḥ śrī-nārāyaṇam ekāyanatayā sāgama-niṣṭham upatiṣṭhamānaḥ suṣṭhu dhyātum ārabdhavān । tatra cāyaṃ janmata eva tan-mayatayā san-matir āsīt । tādṛśa-nandana-lābhānandatas tu tatrāpy atiśayaṃ vindati sma । tataś ca tad-vidha-dhyānāvadhānataḥ samādhim anavadhim āpannavantaṃ taṃ sarvataḥ pracarantaḥ pracetasaś carāḥ sahasā samāsadya sadyaḥ svīya-svāmi-nivāsaṃ praty eva pravāsayāmāsuḥ । eṣa nivāsa-viśeṣaś ca tasya jala-stambha-vidyālambhitāra-bhavān svata eva bhāsvān bhāsvat-kanyā-hrada-stha-vivarasyādhaḥ-pradeśe sadeśa eva rasā-vivara-deśe niveśam āsīdati । na ca kṛṣṇa-prabhāvatā vidita-mahitānubhāvasya tasya tathānayanaṃ nayavatāṃ na sambhāvanīyam । sa hi nirantaram idaṃ cintayati-yad asya mad-bhāgya-jātataḥ sañjātasya sutasya yathottara-prathamāna-mānatayā parama-prema-harṣadam utkarṣaṃ śaśvad eva paśyāma iti । tatas tad evāsakṛd eva yogam āpayituṃ tal-līlāyām upayoga-māyātāyā yogamāyāyā eva samayās ta ete pūtanā-gamanādivat । [] atha tathāveśinam eva vrajeśānaṃ yadā pāśinaḥ puratas tad-ādeśābhiniveśinas te sañcāritavantas, tadā tad-ākārata eva taṃ nirdhārayan punaś ca nārāyaṇa-dhāraṇāvantam avadhārayann ayam atidarādarābhyāṃ kṛta-divya-vastrādi-praśastitayā varaśayyām evādhiśāyayāmāsa । [] svayaṃ ca pitṛ-haraṇāsahiṣṇu-kṛṣṇāgamanam anantaram eva manvānaḥ sudūra-dṛṣṭi-hetuṃ pūr-dvāram adhitiṣṭhann ūrdhvam eva tiṣṭhati sma । [] athātratyaṃ vṛttam anuvṛttyatām । [] yadā khalu kṛṣṇasya tātaḥ kṛṣṇā-pāthasi tan-nāthavattā-mātra-dhanānāṃ janānām adṛśyatām avāpa, tadā diśi diśi kāndiśīkās te jalam avagāhya tad-aprāptitas tad-bāhyaṃ pradeśam āgatāḥ । āgamya ca vikrośanta eva vrajam abhigacchantaḥ, kṛṣṇa-rāmāgraṇyas tān vraja-grāmaṇyaḥ kalitāsukhān svābhimukhān eva lebhire । [] tatra ca vṛtte śruta-mātre parama-duḥkha-pātre sarvataḥ kṛta-mano-virāmau kṛṣṇa-rāmau vikramya sarvam atikramya, paramotkaṇṭhita-matyā jhaṭiti-gatyā pṛthivīm api ghaṭṭayantau, tam eva ghaṭṭam āṭatuḥ । tatra ca kṛṣṇaḥ samagra-vyagram agrajam āliṅgan riṅgad-asram evedam aśrāvayat-bhrātar, mātaram akātaratayābhirakṣya sarva eva rakṣaṇīyāḥ, yāvad ahaṃ pitaram ānīya sukha-vitaraṃ karavāṇi । mātary atrāgatāyāṃ tu na kathañcid api paryāptiṃ paryāpayituṃ śakṣyāmīti । [] tad evaṃ kṛta-saṃvāda-mātraḥ pitaram ānetuṃ nirmita-yātraḥ saṃhanana-bṛṃhita-siṃha-lajjaḥ saṃhita-parikara-sajjaḥ pātāla-vivara-dvāra-pātraṃ sarit-pātram anu mamajja । [] anantaraṃ ca, vrajeśvarī-pradhānāḥ sarva eva tatra caraṇa-mātram ādadhānā rāmam ekam avadhānāḥ kṛṣṇam anusandadhānāḥ papracchuḥ-kva nu yātas tavānujātaḥ? iti । [] sa tu tāṃ vrajendrasudṛśaṃ visadṛśadṛśaṃ parāmṛśann uvāca-mātar, na kātaratām āyāhi । sa tu sampraty eva janakam ādāya svajanasukhaṃ janayi-ṣyati iti । [] atha svamātaram uvāca-hanta, tvam api kathaṃ māṃ hantāsi? mayi viśvāsataḥ śvāsamātraviśiṣṭām etāṃ pāhi । [] tataś ca sarva evānarvāñcaḥ kāliyadamanaprakramatas tadvacanam aklamapramam eva manvānās tāṃ viśramayāmāsuḥ । kintu, vety etat paricetum āpur asakṛd-buddhiṃ na tasmin janāḥ । kintūtkaṇṭhitatāvaguṇṭhita-hṛdāṃ teṣām abhūd vāg iyaṃ hā hā śrī-vrajarāja hā bata hahā śrī-kṛṣṇa kutrāsi bhoḥ? ।। [śārdūla] janī-catuṣṭaya-dhṛtā pluṣṭa-cittā vrajeśvarī ।
śvāsāstitā-tarka-pātraṃ hā hā mātraṃ jagāda sā ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] atha tuṅgācala-jala-cita-suraṅgā-praveśataḥ pracetaḥ-sadana-gatasya tasya vraja-lakṣmī-dayitasya caritam anupacaritam avadhāryatām । [] yada tu te yādasāmpati-bhavanaṃ javataḥ śrī-vraja-rājam abhājayaṃs tadā sa ca tatra sacate sma । yathā ca, dhvānta-dhvāṃsy api tīvratā-śavalanād dṛg-rodhanaṃ dṛg-dvayam ।
kalpāntābhra-taḍid-dhvani-bhrama-dharān vismāpayante sma tān ।।[śārdūlavikrīḍita] [] tataś ca-bilaṃ valamānaḥ sa khalu jambukaḥ kva nu vartate? iti jalpa-kalanayā tasminn avajñā-vardhanasya śrīman-nanda-kula-samardhanasya bhṛśam ardidhiṣati dṛśam ardidiṣati ca tejasi bahula-kolāhala-pravāham avalambamānaḥ sva-gala-valayita-celatayā kṣmāmelita-bhālaḥ sarva-jala-pālaḥ śaṅkita-kaliḥ kalitāñjalir vidūra-bhū-gata evākhaṇḍa-daṇḍavat praṇanāma । [] tasya cedṛśāt kharva-garvatāvalokanāt sarva eva tan-nāthās tathā prathāñcakruḥ । [] tataś ca taruṇāruṇa-kamala-locanaḥ sarva-rocanaḥ karuṇayā puraḥ-saratām āsādya sadyas taṃ varuṇaṃ papraccha-te tu kutra parama-dharmācaraṇā madīya-pitṛ-caraṇāḥ? iti । [] varuṇas tu galita-dhairya-sañjanaḥ sāñjalitayā sāntvaṃ vaco vyānañja-puruṣottama! yatra khalu tatra-bhavāṃs, tatra param asāv asamaḥ parama-mahān sambhavati, nānyatra । kintu teṣām eṣāṃ kiṅkarāṇāṃ kiṃ karavāṇi śāsanam ātmanaś ceti tad anuśāsanam āśāse । [] kṛṣṇaḥ sa-śānta-svāntam āha-varākāṇām eṣāṃ daṇḍaḥ kevalaṃ daṇḍayituṃ pauruṣaṃ khaṇḍayati । avilamba-sparśam eva tu darśayatāt tāta-caraṇa-sarojātam । [] atha yathādiśanti dīrṇa-dīnādīnavās tatra-bhavantaḥ iti । [] vāri-rājaḥ śrī-vraja-rāja-virājamāna-sadana-paryantaṃ panthānaṃ tac-caraṇa-mūlataḥ parama-dukūlānukūlaṃ cakāra, tatra nināya ca gopa-kula-nāyaka-kula-nāyakam । uvāca ca-govinda nīyatām eṣa pitā te pitṛ-vatsala [] iti । [] idam ahaṃ jānāmy eva, tat katham anyathā carāmi? kathaṃ vā parād asya parābhavaḥ syāt? iti bhāvaḥ । [] tad evaṃ varuṇasya pāśād yad bhaya-pātrāyamāṇatvam, tasmād api sva-prabhāveṇa mocakasya tasya- upalabhya ca saurabhyam alabhyasya sutasya saḥ ।
abhyāyayau bahir-vṛttiṃ sabhyānāṃ vismayaṃ vahan ।। [anuṣṭubh] śrīman mukhaṃ tasya ca sandadarśa । svapnāyitaṃ cāsravṛter amaṃsta ।। [indravajrā] [] kṛṣṇas tu tac-caraṇa-yugala-tala-sparśa-pūrvakaṃ tam āliṅgan unnamitavān-tāta, so' ham āgato' smi, ity adhigatavāṃś ca । ] tatra dvayor api samagra-vyagratām āgacchator atha haris tu paritaḥ parīta-para-parīvāra-parīhāsa-śaṅkayā saṅkucita-cittas tatra cātmani ca bāṣpādi-vikāra-vyatiriktākāratām āsādayituṃ vyājahāra-tāta, paritaḥ samavadhīyatām । [] atha vraja-sūtrāmā paritaḥ samīkṣya ca kutrāvām āgatau? iti sa-vailakṣyaṃ putrānanam īkṣate sma । [] sa covāca-tāta, mā tanyatām anyathā-bhāvaḥ । yathāvrajanam eva sva-vrajaṃ vrajiṣyāvaḥ । tataḥ purataś caraṇa-kamalam avadhīyamānam ādhīyatām । [] tatra tu tathā kurvati vyākulatākula-kāku-pūrvaṃ varuṇa uvāca-
kṛpālus tvam aho kṛṣṇa dvayor ekataraṃ kuru । daṇḍaṃ vātha prasādaṃ vā nāparādhaṃ tu śeṣaya ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] tad evaṃ kṛta-yātratayā sthitayor api kṣaṇa-mātram avasthitayos tayor mahopacārāṃś caraṇāgrataḥ samarpitān ācaran praṇāmam ācacāra, cacāla ca sa tābhyāṃ saha yāvad-vivarābhyāsam । āgamya ca tad-abhyāsaṃ tad-vartma-bhāga-sthita-nīraṃ vibhāgam āgamayya tābhyāṃ saha vrajaṃ prati prahita-jana-prahita-mahitālaṅkṛti-mukha-paribarha-sambhṛti-muhūrta-sukha-pūrtitaḥ kṛta-kṛtyaṃ-manyatayā nṛtyann iva nivavṛte । prabhās tad-vartmekṣā-sthita-śithila-jīva-sthiti-daśāḥ ।
gatau dṛṣṭvā bhūyo' py ahaha sukha-tandrīm abhiyayuḥ ।। [śikhariṇī] [] kevalas tu baladevas tāv abhijagāma, praṇanāma ca vraja-rājam । datta-sukha-samāje vraja-rāje tu, tam upagūhya vismṛta-bāhyatayā kiñcana cāsamūhya kṣaṇa-katipayaṃ viramati । punaś ca rāme punaḥ punar namati, rāmānujaḥ sahasā sahasā parikramya parama-ramya-nija-sparśāmṛta-sparśanataḥ prathamaṃ mātaram eva kātaraḥ punar jīva-lokam ālokayāmāsa, kramaśas tv anyam anyam api । milanty api vraja-janatāmilan mithaḥ । parantu tāv akhilam avait parāparam ।। [rucirā]
vādyair nṛtyaiḥ stava-rava-śatair utthite' nyo' nya-marde । ślakṣṇālāpair api samucita-sthāna-niṣṭhaṃ cakāra ।। [śārdūla] yathā-yogyaṃ cānyān vidadhad upaviṣṭān atha balaḥ । kathām etāṃ śṛṇvan paśupa-kulam aśrāvayad api ।। [śikhariṇī]
[] tatrātha datta-svātantryatayā viprān āmantrya paramānnādibhiḥ santarpya tad-abhīpsitāni vīpsayā samarpya, dvādaśyatikrama-bhiyā tat-pravaṇa-dhiyā vratam idam acchidra-pratham astv iti prārthya, gīrbhis tad-āśīrbhis tatra sāmarthyaṃ samartha-kṛtārthaṃ-manyās te dhanyā bahula-kutūhalataḥ sarva eva vrajam āvrajanti sma । [] yatra vrajādhyakṣaḥ svayam adhvānaṃ vrajan, madhye-suta-dvayam abhrājiṣṭa । [] atha kathakas tām etāṃ kathāṃ samāpayan śrī-vrajeśvaraṃ praty āha- pāśi-pāśena sambandhas tvayy āsīn neti kā kathā । tad-bhayenāpi nāsīt tvat-putrasyāsya prabhāvataḥ ।।tad uktaṃ varuṇenāsya karuṇāṃ vīrya-bhīruṇā । govinda nīyatām eṣa pitā te pitṛ-vatsalaḥ ।। iti । [anuṣṭubh]
[] atha dināntare kṛṣṇam antareṇa sabhāntare niviṣṭā gopa-kula-śiṣṭā vraja-patiṃ prati tatratyaṃ citraṃ papracchuḥ । [] sa ca loka-pālasya tasya taṃ mahodayam aihika-lokānām āloka-pathātītam astokaṃ ślokayāmāsa । tatra ca-mitrāṇi, citraṃ śrūyatām iti tad-vāsināṃ kṛṣṇe bhaktim atiriktāṃ varṇayāmāsa । [] tad-varṇanāntaraṃ tu nija-nijam antaram anu vismitānāṃ tasminn īśvaratālambhaka-sambhāvanayā sarveṣām eva seyaṃ bhāvanā-yadi cānaśvara-pratipatti-vaśād ayam īśvaras, tathāpy autpattika-sneha-sampatti-viṣayāśrayatā-maya-nirāmaya-sukha-dāyīti tu sadā mukhya-vyatīta-sarva-tarṣaṃ samutkarṣaṃ draṣṭuṃ suṣṭhu muhur ullasaty eva naś ceto-vṛttiḥ । tac ca kim anena nirbādhaṃ sādhayiṣyate? iti । [] eṣa cāśeṣāṇām eṣāṃ svāpara-paryāya-jñātitayā svābhedena vijñāyamānānām etad abhijñāya, kāruṇya-jāta-yantraṇayā śīghratā-paratantratayā cintitavān- [] aho, ete ca te te mama parama-svajanā, mayi pāramaiśvaryaṃ paryālocya sarvato' py asambhavaṃ mad-vaibhavam anubhavitum icchanti, kintu nānubhavanti yata eva loka-pāla-vaibhava-mātraṃ camatkāra-pātraṃ kurvanti । tādṛśaṃ tad vaibhavaṃ punar eṣāṃ svagati-mayam eva । tat tu tan-mayam api yan nānubhavanti, tat khalv avidyā-kāma-karma-nirmitoccāvaca-gatimati jagati viracitam avatāram anu sarva-sādhāraṇaṃ-manyatayā buddhi-bādhāta eva । sā caiṣām, iti nandādayo gopāḥ kṛṣṇa-rāma-kathāṃ mudā । kurvanto ramamāṇāś ca nāvindan bhava-vedanām ।।[] kṛṣṇe' rpitātma-suhṛd-artha-kalatra-kāmāḥ [] iti । kṛṣṇe kamala-patrākṣe sannyastākhila-rādhasaḥ [] iti ।
ceto viśva-phalāt phalaṃ tvad-aparaṃ kutrāpy ayan muhyati । yad-dhāmārtha-suhṛt-priyātma-tanaya-prāṇāśayās tvat-kṛte ।।[] ity ādibhiḥ pramita-sarvopari-mad-vaśīkāri-prema-mahimnāṃ yadyapi nāvidyādi-mayī, tathāpy eṣām anya-sādhāraṇaṃ-manyatām asahamāno' haṃ madīya-prema-sandoha-maya-mohābhilāṣa-lālanā-jālataḥ sañjāyamānām apy etāṃ tan-mayīm eva manye । [] vastutas tu tādṛśa-premarṇenānādi-kalpata evānyebhyaḥ prattānavakāśām uttamarṇatāṃ gatānām apy eṣāṃ mayy arpita-sarvārthānāṃ gatir eva mama gatis, tad-anugatam eva ca mama paramaṃ vaibhavam, na punar ataḥ param api paraṃ sambhavati । [] tad evaṃ jalāvitur vaibhavād api pitur mama yaś camatkāraḥ, sa tu māṃ duḥkhākaroti । tasmād eteṣāṃ yathā mayi premāveśas tathā naiteṣu mameti tad-anusandhānavatā mayā tad etad eṣām eva vaibhavam eteṣām eva śubhānudhyāna-maya-yogamāyānubhavataḥ sāmpratam enān anubhāvayāni iti । [] tad etad vicintanānantaraṃ dinānantare punar ādi-varāha-purāṇa-vācaka-yācaka-vipra-dvārā-pura-dvārāsthānī-sthitika-vicitra-pitrādy-ābhīra-vīra-pariṣadaṃ prati-kārtika-varti-pūrṇimā-snānam akrūrābhīṣṭa-prade brahma-hrade tūrṇam eva pūrṇa-tat-phalatāṃ sādhayati ity avadhārayan, sāratayā dhārayaṃs tat-prātaḥ sarvāṃs tān dāyādādīn ādāya satrā tatrāgatavān । [] āgatya ca sarveṇa saha tatra nimajjya, tam utsṛjya, tīram āsajya, prakṛtitaḥ paratayā sac-cid-ānanda-ghanaṃ parama-svarūpa-rūpa-rasa-gandha-sparśa-śabdatayātmārāmāṇām apy alabhya-ghanaṃ gopānāṃ sva-niketam etaṃ golokam āvaraka-śaktim apākṛtya vyaktīkṛtavān । [] tiraskariṇīṃ nirākṛtya vicitraṃ divya-citram iva yaṃ khalv asya narākṛti-para-brahmaṇaḥ sva-lokatayā brahmaṇo loka ity ācakṣate । [] yatra kila sveṣām eva madhyam adhyāsitaṃ nija-kula-tilaka-kṛṣṇākāratayā paricitaṃ kṛta-janmādi-gokula-līlā-stuti-śruti-sākṣikatayātiniścitaṃ tam etaṃ sa-lokam ālokayan vraja-lokaḥ sarva-śokaṃ vyatītya, vismayānanda-sandohataḥ pratikṣaṇam eva sukha-saṃroham avāpa । [] tad evaṃ vyajya rajyan-manasas tān vraja-lokān golokataḥ sa daiteyārir daiteyapīḍanādi-krīḍāṃ pūrayituṃ punar vyavadhāpitavāṃś ca । [] atha kathakaḥ samāpanam āha-
īdṛg vrajeśa putras te jita-lokeśa-lokakaḥ । yas tvāṃ ca tava lokaṃ ca lokam etam alokayat ।। [anuṣṭubh] adhi goloke gopāḥ svayam adhi gopeṣu golokaḥ । iti kalayan vanamālī yas taṃ vyānañja taṃ naumi ।। [upagīti]।।
[] tad evaṃ prātaḥ-kathāyāṃ prayātāyāṃ vibhāvarī-kathā vibhāti sma । yathā snigdhakaṇṭha uvāca- tadā rādhādīnāṃ sthitir iha mṛṣā kā prathayitā । na śūnyasya prāptiṃ bhajati paritaḥ kāpi ca daśā ।। [śikhariṇī] tadā śrī-rādhāyāḥ śvasitam amunā sārdham agamat ।
samāgād ity eṣā param iha kavīnāṃ sukavitā ।। [śikhariṇī] ekā rādhām anu tam anu ca snigdha-bhāvā vidagdhā । ceto-vṛtter mukham iva tayor añjasā jāyate sma ।। [śārdūla] lokāntaram antarā sevām ।
sa-sukhāṃ virahān na duḥkhitāṃ tasya ।। [udgīti] ānītāḥ pitṛ-caraṇā vāruṇa-lokāt prananditā lokāḥ । hā rādhā mama śokād bādhā-gīrṇā na jīrṇāsti ।। [āryā] [] atra kākvā jīrṇāsty eveti sambhāvyate । [] tad evaṃ sā tasyāṃ tasminn api rahasi nivedya viśeṣataḥ śrīkṛṣṇam apy upālabdhavatī, yathā-
rāgaṃ vināsti hṛdayaṃ mādhava tava rocate ca tat tubhyam । iti niyataṃ kanakāṅgī pāṇḍū-bhavati sphuṭaṃ rādhā ।। [āryā] yenātidūrād api suṣṭhu kṛṣyate । evam ārdrīkriyate yayā bhavān ।। [upajāti ]
[] madhukaṇṭha uvāca-keyaṃ vṛddhā? yatas tatra nānya-janasya praveśaḥ sambhavatīti pūrvaṃ nirṇītam । [] snigdhakaṇṭhaḥ sahāsam āha-paurṇamāsy eva nānā-veśena tatra praveśatīti । [] atha tadārabhya- agāsīn muralyeti tathyaṃ mṛṣā na । sa vā kaḥ śarair yaś chinatty āśu sarvam ।। [bhujaṅgaprayātā] harir yady apy udyan pratiharitam eva sphuritavān ।
dadhe rādhā-bādhā tad-anadhigamād apy adhikatām ।। [śikhariṇī]।। īdṛśas te patiḥ śyāme yat-kāntes tvaṃ parā gatiḥ । atrābhilāṣaḥ śobhā vā kāntir ity adhigamyatām ।। [anuṣṭubh] ।।
