yadā jātā tarhi pratipadam upāyākṛta-dhiyām । tamaskṛd-viśvasminn ahaha kṛśatā nityam ajani ।। [śikhariṇī] [] tataś ca tad-artham anurahasaṃ nānā-devatām arthayamānā vyartham iva bhramanti sma । vrajeśitroḥ sadma vāsaḥ paraṃ śvasuratānayoḥ ।
kṛṣṇa eva patir bhūyān mama janmani janmani ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] tataś ca kadācit kālindīm anu parasparaṃ vindamānā babhūvuḥ । bhavati samantād bahūnāṃ cet । milanaṃ ghaṭate yathā sa-tīrthānām ।। [udgīti]
[] militānāṃ tāsāṃ parasparaṃ hārdam api jātam । tathā hi- diśi diśi jātāḥ snigdhā vyatimilitāḥ suṣṭhu bibhrati sneham । medura-mudira-samūhe muhur api yasmāt tathā dṛṣṭam ।। [āryā] [] tatra jāte cāsauhārde hārdam api parasparaṃ vyaktam । yataḥ-
hṛdayaṃ vyaktiṃ mitho yāti । vada tarhi syāt pidhānaṃ kim? ।। [upagīti] [] tataś ca parasparaṃ hṛd-bāṣpam udgīrṇavatīnāṃ dṛg-bāṣpam api vikīrṇavatīnāṃ tāsāṃ daśānta-daśāvaśāṅgatayā sambhāvyamānānām anukṣaṇaṃ sukhā-kāṅkṣiṇī pārikāṅkṣiṇī-veśa-viśeṣaṃ vindamānā tatra vṛndā gatā । [] sā hy evaṃ purā cintitavatī-rāga eva khalv āsāṃ vrajanāgarasya tasya samāgamāya vāgagocaraśaktibhāg avasīyate ।
[] rāgaś ca loka-rīti-maya-praṇayata eva jāgarūkatayā garīyān varīvartīti devatāntarārādhanam eva sādhayitavyam, na tu tad-ārādhanam iti । [] athāgamya ca tat-kṛtābhivādana-sva-kṛtābhivadana-vidhau labdha-vidhau sābhidadhāti sma-[] aham atraiva vane vasantī bhavatīnāṃ bhāvavatīnām avasthāḥ paśyantī dayā-vidīrṇa-hṛdayā samāyātāsmi । tad iyaṃ mama siddhā vidyā sva-karṇānubiddhā vidhīyatām । nātiprayāsa-bhāvitatā ca bhavatīnāṃ bhavitā, kintu māsa-mātram atra śramābhāsaḥ । [] sā khalu mantra-mayī yogamāyā mayā dayāvatī sādhitāstīti । [] tad evaṃ tāsāṃ karṇa-vivaram anu mantra-varṇān nidhivan nidhāya tad-vidhim api sa-vidhim abhidhāya mudāntar-hitavatī sāntarhitavatī । tataś ca tās tad-upadeśa-lagnāḥ parama-sukha-magnā babhūvuḥ । yataḥ- prāpnoty eṣa tu yogya-kalpam atha ced dhatte sad-ullāsitām ।
pūjyā mantra-varaś ca vāñchita-dharas tāsām itaḥ kiṃ sukham? ।। [śārdūla] [] ataevāmūr viśramya mārgaśīrṣīya-śirṣāyāmāṇatā-labhya-pratipadam ārabhya saṃgatya vratam ārabdhavatyaḥ । yatrāruṇa-kṛtāruṇa-guṇa-prasaram avasaram anu parasparaṃ gṛha-visarataḥ samākāraṇāparā vyatibaddha-karā yamunā-gamana-tat-parā gāna-parāyaṇā babhūvuḥ; yatra paraspara-parīhāsa-prāyatayā nijābhiprāyaṃ vyañjayāmāsuḥ । yathā- tvām upayantā sakhi vanamālī । sakala-śubhākara-vara-guṇa-śālī ।।
vārtāṃ cālayitā sukha-sacitām ।। sukham ayitārau kṛta-dhana-vitarau । sakhibhir narmaṇi yaḥ kopayitā ।। veśaṃ dhāsyati sa nijavivāhe ।
ghana-capalābhirucām iva mūlam ।। citra-pracchada-ruci-parivītam । alakāvali-maṇi-citraka-bhājam ।। tāmbūla-cchavi-jid-adhara-surāgam ।
graiveyakam anukṛta-maṇi-melam ।। āvāpaka-dhṛti-valayita-śastam । vanamālādika-mālya-samājam ।। caraṇa-vibhūṣaṇa-gaṇa-ruci-magnam ।
yat tu na dṛṣṭaṃ kvacana ca pūrvam ।। sarvābharaṇaṃ svayam iti garvam । kalayiṣyanti suhṛdbhir upetam ।। kusumair varṣiṣyanti sagītam ।
mudam āpsyati sa svayam api tena ।। dhṛtam api yatnād bhavitā bhittam । sakhi visṛjeḥ sukha-mūrcchā-veśam ।। tatir api gāsyati bimboṣṭhī ।
gāli-prāyaṃ tad api ca gānam ।। kartāras te sa-kusuma-vṛṣṭim । sukha-sammardo bhavitā rāme ।। narma-kutūhalam udayed varatanu ।
āneṣyanti tvām iha sahanidhi ।। sthāpayitāraḥ priyaratipātrīm । grāhayitā varakaram anu sajalam ।। kim bhaviteti jñātā kena? ।
kṛtam iva paśyāmy amunā kamanam ।। ।। । [mātrāsamakā] [] tad evaṃ yamunāṃ prāpya drutam eva gānaṃ samāpya velāyāṃ bālya-cāpalyena kalye projjhita-celā eva mithaḥ kṛta-melā velāyāṃ nimajjanti sma । nimajjya ca-kauṣeyatayā kṣālanāṃ vināpi na pariheyam iti tad eva celaṃ paridhāya sevyāyā devyāḥ saikatām arcām arcitāṃ vidhāya mantram anusandhāya dhāma samāyānti sma । [] tad evaṃ tāvan māsaṃ yāvad vidhāya tat-pūraka-dinaṃ vratasyāpi pūrakaṃ jātam iti paramānanda-pūraṇataḥ sūrajā-pūram anu dūranirjanatā-jāta-nirvrīḍatayā kṣaṇam akrīḍan । [] tad evaṃ pūrva-pūrvaṃ jānan vraja-rāja-nandanas tuṣṭa-manāḥ kumāra-catuṣṭayam anuvidhaṃ vidhāya tatra prasthāya guptam upta-cittatayā tāḥ paśyati sma ।
[] ye khalu dāma-sudāma-vasudāma-kiṅkiṇi-saṃjñās tasya prajñāhaṅkāra-citta-manasāṃ bahiḥ-prakāśatayā labdha-samajñās tantra-vijñātṛbhir vijñāyante, ta ete hi kumārā jāta-catuḥ-pañca-varṣāḥ paraspara-savayaskatā-dhṛta-harṣāḥ kṛṣṇād anudinam āsādita-prema-varṣāś calanārambhata eva-kutra yāmaḥ? iti pṛcchanta eva gacchantaḥ kṛta-tat-saṅgam āgacchanti sma । tad evaṃ- āgamya tatra kara-vārita-tat-prahāsaḥ । sadyas tad-aṃśuka-cayaṃ sa harir jahāra ।। [vasantatilakā] pūrvaṃ sa-ḍimbha-nikaraḥ sphuṭam ujjahāsa ।
vargaḥ samaṃ sabhayam ūrdhvita-dṛṣṭir āsīt ।। [vasanta] hāsaṃ taṃ paricitya bālya-valitās tāḥ prekṣya cānyo' nyataḥ । kṛtvā nīcam udakta-vaktram udake nyak-cakrire padminīḥ ।। [śārdūla-vikrīḍitam] atalina-nalina-vanānāṃ bhramam iha cakrur mukhāni tāsāṃ na ।
hemante tad-ayogāt kintu nyak-kāram evātra ।। [āryā] punar udayati śīte' drākṣur etāḥ kadambam । punar avṛtim ayāsīc cātma-lakṣāya tābhiḥ ।। [mālinī] syārūḍha-nīpaka-taroḥ sahasā dṛg-antaḥ ।
yāsāṃ ca nīrabhṛti cātakarītim āpa ।। [vasantatilakā] uccakair jahasur bālāś cukruśus tatra bālikāḥ । ūcuś cedaṃ tu vaḥ kṛtyaṃ vrajādṛtyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। [anu] [] atha kṛṣṇena muhur api śikṣitā bālāḥ procuḥ ।
kṛtyaṃ vā kim akṛtyaṃ vā na vidmo vayam aṇv api । śikṣārthaṃ kintu vaḥ prāptā vīkṣyājñāsiṣma tat punaḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] yaḥ kaścic chikṣakas tasmād bhavadbhiḥ suṣṭhu śikṣitam । abhyasyatha vraje tac ca sva-guror māna-vṛddhaye ।। [anuṣṭubh]
kimartho' yam upālambhas tan na vidmas tu kiñcana । bhavatyo jala-cāriṇyo vayaṃ vṛkṣāgra-gāminaḥ ।। [anu] vikrāntir luṇṭhatāṃ yogyā yad vaḥ śākhāgragāmitā । dīnatā luṇṭhitānāṃ syād yan naḥ salilagāhitā ।। [anu]
ambaram apy ambaratām āsādayituṃ tavāsti sāmarthyam । iha dāmodara cauryaṃ kiyad iva śauryaṃ samarpayatu? ।। [āryā] [] atha kṛṣṇaḥ sa-smayam āha sma-na nagnā etāḥ pāthasi magnāḥ । tad idaṃ tu mayā parihasitam eva । dṛṣṭaṃ bhavadbhir duṣṭhu-prakṛtīnām ākṛti-mātra-suṣṭhutā-yutānām āsām anuṣṭhitam; yan madīyāny eva śastāni vastrāṇi vihārataḥ samasta-vyastatayā yatra tatra visrastāni । tāny etā daridrāṇāṃ kanyāḥ sphuṭam anyāyatayā paricitya ca vicitya paridadhānā, mādṛśas tu dṛśaḥ sakāśād gopanaṃ kāmayamānā bāḍhaṃ jalam evāvagāḍhāḥ । yāni khalv atisvacchānāṃ tigma-cchavi-kanyā-jalānām antar apracchannāny eva lakṣyante, yāny eva cāsāṃ jala-magna-pratyaṅga-lagnāni svarṇa-savarṇa-varṇāni varṇā iva nirvarṇyante । tasmāt plavanta eva bhavantaḥ pratyekam etāḥ kara-gṛhīta-karāḥ samānayantām । [] tad etad avadhārya tīra-paryantam avatīrya sambhrama-pratīkṣitālpa-kālān kṛṣṇājñā-pālān bālān amūḥ pratyūcuḥ-[] kathaṃ stambham avalambadhve? niḥśaṅkam eva saṅkrāmata ।
[] sakhīḥ prati ca prāvocan-atraivānīya pānīya-vāsa-sukhaṃ luṇṭhākān etān ākuṇṭham āsādayata । āhara-vasanām āhara- vanitāṃ yasmāt kriyāṃ sadādhīdhve । kātyāyanī-prasādāt tam api vikarṣāma toyāntaḥ ।। [āryā] [] atha tad etac chrutavanta eva drutavantaḥ skhalanta iva nīpa-tarv-antam āsadya sadyas tam eva tarum āruruhuḥ ।
[] kṛṣṇas tu sa-hāsaṃ spaṣṭam idam abhyacaṣṭe-aho, śubhaṃyūyamānānām āsām ahaṃyutā bhavatīnāṃ bhavatu, paśyāmas tatra-bhavatīṣu devatā-prabhāvam । yāvad eva tad etam udavāsam urīkṛtya bhavatyas tiṣṭhanti, tāvad vayam api dhṛta-niṣṭhās taror upariṣṭād eva nabho-vāsam urarīkṛtya tiṣṭhāma । na nādeya-bhayaṃ tasya tarau yasya bhavet sthitiḥ । pātra-sātkṛta-gātrāṇāṃ pṛcchyā nādeyatā punaḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] aho, hima-śratha-ślathāṅga-sandhayaḥ parama-durbalāḥ ! sarvābhir evārvāg āgamyatām ।
[] kṛṣṇa uvāca-vanadevatayā hṛtaṃ mayā tu prasahya tasyāḥ samāhṛtaṃ vāsaḥ samāsādyatām । [] tad etad uktvāntar-vāriṇa eva prasārita-karāḥ kiñcid abhyānañcuḥ । kṛṣṇas tu sāṅguli-vyaṅgam uvāca-aye śata-patra-patra-netrāḥ ! savidhe' trāgamyatām । [] kṛṣṇa uvāca-mama dṛṣṭir visṛṣṭiś ca viśiṣṭatām āpnoti' iti । [] kṛṣṇa uvāca-grahaṇātivṛttir vastra-parivṛttiś ca na syāt ।
[] tāś ca parasparam ūcuḥ-aho mugdhāḥ! vañcayitum eveyaṃ prapañcanā । [] kṛṣṇas tu tāḥ sandarśya jihvāṃ sandaśya babhāṣe-satyam evedaṃ bravīmi, nāsatyam । [] tāḥ punaḥ pratyūham ūhamānā vyatyūcuḥ-aho, mūḍha-buddhayaḥ ! suvyaktāntar-nigūḍha-hāsaḥ parīhāsa evāyam asya । [] kṛṣṇas tu gūḍham api smitam agūḍha । samūḍha-priya-vadyatayāpy avādīt-hanta, nahi nahi, yasmād vrata-kṛśatayā bhṛśa-dayā-viṣayā eva yūyam, na tu dūyamānatām arhatha ।
spṛhayāluś cānya-vastraṃ gṛhayāluś ca yaḥ sa tu । śītaluṣu dayāluś ced āścaryātiśayālutā ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] bhavatu । visrabdhaṃ vadata, kadā satyaṃ vaktum ārabdhaṃ tatra-bhavadbhiḥ? [] kṛṣṇa uvāca-kadāpi nānṛtaṃ vacasi kṛtavān asmi ।
[] tā sahāsam ūcuḥ-satyam ete bhavataḥ prāpta-marmāṇaḥ sa-dharmāṇaś ca dṛśyante । [] kṛṣṇa uvāca-hanta, muṣṭi-sambadhya-madhyamāḥ, pratītim atītha cet pratyakṣata eva lakṣyatām । sarvābhir evāgamya na vā sarvān atirekayā kayācid ekayāpi । bālāḥ prema-pariplutāḥ । jāta-hāsā na niryayuḥ ।। [] iti ।
nīre ca śītam ity ubhayam । imās tatraiva kiñcid abruvata ।। [anu] vraja-jana-mahanīyaś cāsi yācāmahe tat । vitara vitara vāsaś cānayaṃ mā ca kārṣīḥ ।। [mālinī]
[] kṛṣṇa uvāca-mamānayaṃ ko vā nayana-viṣayaḥ kṛtaḥ? pratyuta sat-kula-prabhavatīnāṃ bhavatīnāṃ vana-devatāhṛta-vastrāṇāṃ sāhāyyam eva kāryam iti tathā mayārabdham asti । na tu bhavatīnāṃ cela-cela-pracaye mādṛśām abhilāṣa-melaḥ sambhavati । tasmād asmat-paritoṣa-poṣaṇāya yadi kiñcid api dattha, tadā tan-madād eva devatā-virodham apy anurodha-viṣayī-kurmaḥ । [] atha tad etad evam avadhāritavatyaḥ kātyāyanī-vratavatyas tad etan manasi vicāritavyaḥ-hanta, yad asmābhir manasi rañjitaṃ, tad evāyaṃ vyañjitaṃ kartuṃ prayatate । tasmād asmākam ayam eva samayaḥ । kintu kim api lakṣyam evātra lakṣyam, tad api svata eva labdham yat pṛthu-śīta-bhītatādikam atra prakaṭam eva ghaṭate । [] atha taṃ prāhuḥ-hā, hā, drutam anena haimanena pavanena śīta-parītatayā jīvana-viparītatāṃ vayam āyātāḥ, tasmān marma-bhedakaṃ narma vṛthā mā kṛthāḥ, kintu vastram eva sevaya । yad vā vāñchasi, tat tu lāñchanam aṅgīkṛtyāpi kariṣyāmaḥ । [] kṛṣṇaḥ sa-smitam uvāca-hanta, yadi madiṣṭaṃ dāsyatha, tarhi dāsyam eva svīkuruta ।
[] atha tāś cintayāmāsuḥ-hanta, sahasā marma-sparśe karmaṭhatām eva labdhavān asau । bhavatu, vayam api narmāśritya tad eva śarmāṅgī-kurmaḥ । [] kṛṣṇaś ca sa-smitam āha sma-tatra ca yan mamoditam, tad anumoditaṃ purataḥ kuruta । [] atha tāḥ parasparam ālocana-pūrvaṃ nikocita-locanam ūcuḥ-bhavatu, karavāma tavoditam iti । [] tad evam api kṛṣṇe sa-tṛṣṇe' pi tuṣṇīm eva sthite punar ūcuḥ-dehi vāsāṃsi dharmajña iti ।
[] atra cānyathā nijāṅgīkāra-sabhaṅgī-bhāvād dharma eva marma-bādhāyāṃ nātmānaṃ saṃvarmayed iti bhāvaḥ । [] tathāpi tathā sthite tasmin kautuka-nigūḍha-smite punar ūcuḥ-no ced rājñe bruvāmahe' iti । [] atra ca bhaya-nirmuktam imaṃ tad-yukta-mātram ācaritum uktam idaṃ na tu vastutaḥ । [] tad eṣa vyāja-padena rāja-padena yaṃ viśeṣam abudhyate, tam eva budhyatāṃ nāma nikāmam ity abhiprāyaḥ ।
[] kṛṣṇaś ca tad-upayuktam uktavān-aho, kadā dāsyo bhaviṣyatha? kadā vā mayoditaṃ kariṣyatha? tat tu nopalabhāmahe । yadi vettham satyam eva, tadā gaty-antaram antarā, jalād utthāya sarva-sampad utthāya smitena sametam eva sameta, na tu sūkṣmayāpi rukṣatayā । na cen, mithyā-saṅkalpa-jalpānāṃ tata evādharma-marma-kalpānāṃ sāhāyyam asmābhiḥ kathaṃ vā prathanīyam? [] tathāpi tāsām anutthānam uṭṭaṅkya kaṭhinatā-ghaṭitam ācaṣṭe-na vayaṃ vṛthā kṛtāśānāṃ kanyā-pāśānāṃ vaḥ sambandham anurundhmahe । kintu- idaṃ ca me dayālutvam eva budhyadhvam añjasā । no cen nāhaṃ pradāsye kiṃ kruddho rājā kariṣyati? ।। [anuṣṭubh]
[] atra ca rāja-padaṃ vyājāya vyājahāra । tataś ca maunaṃ pratilabhya tāsāṃ bhayam upalabhya, tena karuṇa-sabhya-śiromaṇinā pratyayam ācarya, kathañcit pratyaye cācarite śītārtatā-nirvarti-vārtatām āhartuṃ vrīḍā-niviḍa-jaḍa-vapuṣo' pi jaḍād utterur iti vārtayanti । tad yadi tathā syāt tadā vastutas tu tat-kāraṇam idam astu- ।। MISSING! dehaṃ no cen no' ti samayasya yaiva sīmā । nirvastrā gati-vidhaye himaṃ tu lakṣyam ।। [praharṣiṇī]
[] tad evaṃ kathañcid udakād uktāś ca tā na vyaktāvayavā jātāḥ । kintu- keśa-vistṛti-dhṛtāparāmbarāḥ । kubjikāvad amilan kumārikāḥ ।। [rathoddhatā] [] tataś ca-paśya kṛṣṇa, paśya sarvatas trastā etā loptrāṇi vastrāṇi pāthasy eva srastāni vidhāyāgatā iti saṃlapya prabala-hāsaṃ valgati bāla-varge, haris tv idaṃ bhāvitavān atīva dayām ayāmāsa । yathā-
śaśadhara-tanvā tulanām āhata-lakṣaṇatayā yayur yad api । tad api ca tāṃ sahasāmūr āhata-lakṣaṇatayā jigyuḥ ।। [āryā] na vrīḍākṣayam evam apy atha daśām etāṃ gatā mat-puraḥ । utkaṇṭhā kiratī viloṭhayati mām āsāṃ nijāśarmaṇi ।। [śārdūla]
[] tathāpy āsāṃ suṣṭhu tan-niṣṭhāṃ niṣṭaṅkayituṃ paṅka-darśinaṃ mano-ratha-sparśinaṃ parihāsam apy atīva spaṣṭayituṃ cittam idam utkaṇṭhate । yadā gatā api saṅkocāvagāhataḥ parasparam āhata-prakāśāvayavā eva tiṣṭhanti iti । [] prakāśayann uvāca-are re, capalāḥ, kathaṃ bhavanto hasanti? etāḥ khalu nagnikā eva kathaṃ nagnikā-bhāve doṣam arhanti?iti । [] atha punar vastra-kadambaṃ kadamba-skandha-sandhi-viśeṣe sa-pratyāhāraṃ tat-pratyakṣa-saṃvalitatayā sandhāya prema-bandhāya sa-smitaṃ tāḥ praty evam āha sma-[] dāsyāṅgīkāra-kāraṇāt pradāsyāmy eva tāny etāni vastrāṇi । kintu pūrvam aśakya-nirṇayaḥ, samprati tu nirvarṇya nirṇītaḥ, so' yaṃ sad-guruto yajata-namatāṃ prāptavatīnāṃ bhavatīnāṃ durnayaḥ sapadi māṃ vivarṇayan vartate । tad etad avadhāryatāṃ bhavatībhiḥ- yat tad eva jaladevahelanam ।
śīrṣabhākkarayugaṃ sa namyatām ।। [rathoddhatā] [] tās tu tatra sāpatrapa-cittāś ca parama-bhīti-bhittās tathākāryatayāvadhārya paśyata ke' pi śabdāyante iti bālānāṃ dṛṣṭīḥ pratārya patir eva devatā iti vicārya sa-parihāsa-vilāsa-vyājatas tam eva namaścakruḥ-svāmin, namas tubhyam iti । [] tataś ca kṛṣṇaḥ sa-kautuka-tṛṣṇayā tāsāṃ prati pratīkaṃ sandṛśya, snigdhatāṃ vidagdhatām api parāmṛśya, labdha-prasāda-melaḥ khelā-valitaṃ celāni yathāsvam arpayāmāsa । yatra ca-dṛṣṭi-patha-sevanād eva bhavatīnāṃ puṣṭi-dīrghatādikaṃ mama muṣṭi-gataṃ jātaṃ, katham anyathā samarpaṇaṃ kuryām? ity evaṃ tuṣṭiṃ dadānaḥ sva-vicakṣaṇatāṃ lakṣayāmāsa । kintu- ānukūlyam abhigamya śarmadam ।
pratyuta pramadayām babhūva tāḥ ।। [rathoddhatā] tarhi svāṅga-vṛtiṃ dadhur muhur aho vyaktāntaraṅgārati । tatrāgād vraja-subhruvām ahaha bhoḥ kāmasya vāmā gatiḥ ।। [śārdūla] ।। MISSING!
bhṛṅga-śreṇya ivāmbhojaṃ rasa-pūrṇaṃ kumārikāḥ । bhartṛ-kāmās tadā kṛṣṇaṃ varītuṃ paritaḥ sthitāḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] atha teṣu cākarāleṣu bāleṣu-cala cala kiṃvā karaṇīyam atra? iti kara-dvayaṃ vasanādi-parikara-cayaṃ cākṛṣya hṛṣyatsu vitaraṇīyaṃ varam ambara-hāritāhārī hariḥ svam anusaṃhitavān । tataś ca- tāsāṃ vijñāya gopālaḥ sva-kara-sparśa-kāmyayā ।
dhṛta-vratānāṃ saṅkalpaṃ kalpayāmāsa siddhidam ।। [anuṣṭubh] mayy āviṣṭa-manās tv anādaram athācaryātra mā bādhayati । saṃkalpo nirupadhir eṣa bhavatīṣv evātisatyo mataḥ ।। [śārdūla] vasyante svayam eva bījavad amūs tanvanti nānya-spṛhām ।
kintu syād rasanīyarūpam iti ced yuṣmākam āstāṃ kathā ।। [śārdūla] pare te te dharmāḥ sa punar udabodhi svayam iha । kṣapāyāṃ kasyāñcit kila milanam apy āśu bhavitā ।। [śikhariṇī] [] tad evaṃ tābhyaḥ pratiśrutavati tasminn adhikam eva tāsām āveśo jātaḥ । yathāha śrī-śukaḥ-
ity ādiṣṭā bhagavatā labdha-kāmāḥ kumārikāḥ । dhyāyatyas tat-padāmbhojaṃ kṛcchrān nirviviśur vrajam ।।[] iti । ūrubhyāṃ jānu-yugmāt pada-sarasi-ruha-dvandvam āpur murāreḥ । dṛṣṭaṃ padaṃ tu pratipadam udabhūd antare lagnam āsām ।। [sragdharā]
dve cittavāsasī nītvā kumārīṇāṃ paraṃ dade । na pūrvaṃ tu nirākāraṃ gopanīyam atīva saḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] vismṛtya vrajam eva jagmur abhavaṃs tenaiva pūrṇa-kriyāḥ । kṛṣṇāṅgī-kṛti-śarma ced vavalire kiṃ śiṣṭam iṣṭaṃ param? ।। [śārdūla]
nāsmad arcanam iti pratipadya । kintu rāga-viṣayaḥ svayam eva ।। [svāgatā] [] madhukaṇṭha uvāca-nūnam etāś ca gargeṇaiva govindād apetāḥ kṛtāḥ । [] snigdhakaṇṭha uvāca-kṛtāḥ, kintu na sākṣāt ।
[] snigdhakaṇṭha uvāca-yadyapi sādhvī-śiromaṇi-ramaṇīnāṃ rādhādīnāṃ dīnāyamānānām ālocana-saṅkocatas tasya punar vrajāgamanam anu mano na jātaṃ, tathāpi tad-anusandhānaṃ vinā vrata-bandhādi-dvayaṃ na sandhātavyam iti śrī-vraja-pati-jampatyoḥ kṛta-nibandhatayā, rādhādīnāṃ vadhūnām ābhād utpanna-manaskāra-pratibandhatayā ca tāḥ parasparayā parākṛtāḥ । [] snigdhakaṇṭha uvāca-bahiḥ kaumāreṇa rahas tu śrī-hari-pariṇītatā-vyavahāreṇa । [] madhukaṇṭha uvāca-satyaṃ, bālyam eva khalu pūrvāsāṃ bodhasya virodhaṃ kurvāṇam āsīd iti viparīta-rītir jātā । katham iva jñānottarāṇām āsāṃ sā bhavet? iti । evaṃ balānujātena yad vilambāvalambanam ।
tad balaṃ balavaj jātaṃ tava saṃvalanaṃ vinā ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] yata eva pūrvaṃ stabdhā veṇu-śikṣā ena punar ārabdhā । yatra kathā-viśeṣa-prathanaṃ padya-dvayaṃ sāmprata-līlā-mayam api, śaradu-dāśaye sādhujāta [] ityādivat tāsāṃ vacasā rasāvahaṃ syād iti tad-dvārā śrī-parīkṣic-chikṣā-guruṇā nikṣiptaṃ, tad yathā- datta-kṣaṇaṃ kvacid araṇya-jana-priyasya । sthātuṃ tvayābhiramitā bata pārayāmaḥ ।।[]
iti tāsāṃ rāsa-rajany-ārambhe dainya-saṃvedanaṃ nivedanam । śrī-kuṅkumena dayitā-stana-maṇḍitena । limpantya ānana-kuceṣu juhus tad-ādhim ।।[] iti pūrva-varṇita-veṇu-varṇana-mayam ।
[] tad idaṃ sparśa-dvitayaṃ kānta-yogaja-bhoga-viśeṣam ayaṃ na syāt, rāsa-rajanyāṃ vakṣyamāṇa-kṛṣṇa-pratyākhyānāyukteḥ । rāsārambha eva bhagavān api rantuṃ manaś cakre [] ity ukteś ca । [] tad evaṃ tvayābhiramitā [] ity asya tu tat-sparśānantaraṃ tvayā sarvato-bhāvena prayukta-raty-ākhya-bhāvā ity evārthaḥ saṅgacchate । [] tasmād athedaṃ vivriyate । tad evaṃ dīrgha-rātratayā mandatā-pātraṃ hemantārdhena sārdhaṃ śiśiraṃ niśi niśi vaṃśī-śaṃsitam abhyasyati tasmin vasanta āyātaḥ । vasantati nidāgho' pi vasantasyātra kiṃ bruve ।
vasantaṃ yatra govindaṃ sarva-santaḥ sadā viduḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] tathāpi hemanta-śiśirāv api tāpad-āpad-āyatanatayā yasya yāsāṃ ca pratibhāsate sma । tathā ca tāsāṃ kṛṣṇa-kṛṣṇa-preyasīnāṃ pratyekaṃ bhāvanā, ṛtūnām anyāyaṃ bata kathayitāsmīti laṣitam । vitarjann evāsmān akṛta-vṛjinā dhik praviśati ।। [śikhariṇī]
dvirepho barbaraḥ proktaḥ para-puṣṭaś ca ceṭakaḥ । tau cāgraṇyau madhor dṛṣṭau yāpyatā kāpy ataḥ kim u? ।। [anuṣṭubh] pikāḥ parama-pañcamaṃ madhu-lihāṃ ganāś cumbanam । bhaved ahaha naḥ samaṃ sapadi mādhavīyair vṛtam ।। [pṛthvī]
ṛturājaḥ praṇāyyo' yaṃ nyāyyam atra na vidyati । prapalāyya kva vā yāmaḥ śyāmaṃ naḥ sa tu karṣati ।। [anuṣṭubh] jvālāḥ kiṃśuka-sañcayā diśi vidiśy aṅgāra-sārāḥ pikāḥ । hā hā kṛṣṇa-ghanaṃ vinā kathaya ko nistāra-vistārakaḥ? ।। [śārdūla]
ayam atha melayiteti sampratītiḥ । sphuṭam anayatvam ṛtoḥ sahate ko vā? ।। [puṣpitāgrā] rādhā rādhā-padaṃ māsi mādhave vidhutāṃ vidhuḥ । priyā-saṅga-kṛte labdhuṃ paurṇamāsīm avaikṣata ।। [anu]
dvijānāṃ kākalī tatra viyoge yāga-sammite । ajani vrajatanvīnāṃ dhāyyevāgni-samindhanī ।। [anu] sahante śaśino jvālāṃ vāyoḥ kṣveḍaṃ pibanti ca । rādhādayo mahābādhā vaiyagryād vrajanāyaka ।। [anu]
vṛndāvane tamālas tvam ahaṃ campakavallikā । agayor nau mithaḥ saṅgo vṛndayaiva na cānyathā ।। [anu] [] tac ca dṛṣṭvā muhur api nayanābhyāṃ spṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaḥ sa-tṛṣṇam idam acintayat-[] hanta, bhadrāṃ padmāṃ nityam āgacchann api bhadrāṃ padmām adyāpi nāgacchann asmi । śyāmalābhā-madhuratām añcann api śyāmalābhilāṣa-vidhuratām añcann asmi । nakhara-vijita-candrāvalīkatām āpnuvann api candrāvalīṃ prati labdha-tṛṣṇatām āpnuvann asmi । [] hanta hanta, yadyapy evam evam, tathāpi krama-prāpta-sulalita-viśākhānvita-rādhatāṃ āvrajann apy alabdha-sulalita-viśākhānvita-rādhatāṃ yadāvrajāmi, tad idaṃ mām atiduḥkhākaroti । tasyā rādhāyā eva nūnam iyaṃ vidagdhatā-nidagdha-buddheḥ paṭīyasī paripāṭī iti ।
[] atha mādhava-pūrṇimām āsājya, sarvato virajya ca, pūrṇa-śikṣā-vilakṣaṇaṃ-manyamanā mādhavaḥ kiñcana durgamaṃ gahanam avagāhamānaḥ parama-muralī-dhamana-līlayā dhairyam ūnayann, amūḥ pradhūyanati sma; muhuḥ pradharṣayann ākarṣati sma ca, sādhāraṇatayā rādhāpi samāgamiṣyatīti । [] rādhā tu tatra dvitra-praharaṃ citravad evāsīn na punar ākṛṣṭatām avaliṣṭa pūrvam anyeṣām ākarṣaṇe tā iva । [] atha śrī-vanamāli-śāli vṛndāvanam indranīla-kāntibhir valitam iva dṛśā, yamunā-jala-paramāṇubhiḥ paricitam iva tvacā, mṛgamada-parāgaiḥ sa-rāgam iva nasā vicārya, tābhir viveśa । tataś ca- paṅktis tad-vṛddhi-saṅkhyā-miti-rahitatamās tatra yātāḥ samantāt ।
tac-chrī-vaktraṃ nirīkṣya pratihata-matayaḥ śarmalīnā babhūvuḥ ।।[sragdharā] [] tataḥ sa-maryādāś ca tāḥ sahasā hareḥ samaryādaṃ sajjamānā lajjayā tatrāvahitthām apy avalambamānās tasya caraṇa-spṛṣṭi-prathamakaṃ dṛṣṭi-patham adhitiṣṭhanti sma । tatra ca- yadyapi murahara-purataḥ kiñcana na vyañjitaṃ tābhiḥ । tad api vilakṣaṇam evāprathayad amūṣāṃ vilakṣaṇaṃ bhāvam ।। [udgīti]
[] tad evaṃ sa ca samātmane tiṣṭhamānā goṣṭha-ramaṇīr nirīkṣya kṣaṇa-katipayaṃ tal-lakṣmī-niṣṭha-manā āsīt । [] paścāt tu rādhikā-sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ vinā nirjanāraṇyam api saṅgatās tā bhaṅgī-viśeṣād anaṅgī-kurvaṃś cārvaṅgīr āyatyām aṅgīkāra-kāraṇāvadhāraṇāñci kiñcid vyañjanayā rañjayann iva kañja-nayanaḥ punar akṛta-spṛhāya ca gṛhāya prahāpayāmāsa । tasmād bhavatyaḥ kila saṅgatā iha । śaṅke tataḥ suṣṭhv iti nātra tiṣṭhata ।। [upajāti ] iti ।
kuruta mayi na kiṃ vaḥ prītim apy asmi vedmi । bhavad-abhimata-siddhiṃ svena śīghraṃ dadhīta ।। [mālinī] iti । nātṛpat karuṇā-dṛṣṭir nātrāpsīt prāpitā śrutiḥ । nātārpsīt prārcchitā nāsā nātarpīd arpitaṃ manaḥ ।। [anu]
[] tad evaṃ gītaṃ, yarhy ambujākṣa [] ityādi । [] rādhāyāṃ tu tatra yāma-dvayaṃ cetanā-virāmataḥ prāpta-bādhāyāṃ bandhu-samavāye ca nivṛtta-sarvopāye, tūrṇam eva tad-abhyarṇaṃ pūrṇimā vṛndayā saha vindamānā babhūva । vindamānā ca kaṣṭa-bhāg atispaṣṭam ācaṣṭa- [] yadi mad-uṭaja-kuṭajam etām ekākinīṃ yāma-mātrāyāmam avasaraṃ vāsayatha, tadā mayā nātivirāmayā pratikartavyam iti । [] tataś ca sarva-sammatyā katham api jātayā tasyās tatra saṅgatyā sphurad-atyāveśa-maṅgalā madhumaṅgalena śārṅgiṇam ānāyitavatī । ānāyya cāsanādinā sabhājya smita-sphurad-upālambhaṃ sambhāṣate sma-bhavatu, bhavatā yat kṛtaṃ tat kṛtam eva । samprati tatra sampratipattiṃ vidhehi ।
[] paurṇamāsī uvāca-ārtānām asmākaṃ bahu-vārtā na vārtatvāya vartate, kintu nija-mūrti-sparśatas tasyā mūrtim apasāraya । jñāyate na jaladena tena cet । gopyate kim iti sā muhur muhuḥ? ।। [rathoddhatā] [] paurṇamāsī tu smitvā tasya mukhaṃ paśyantī kṛṣṇa-mukhaṃ paśyati sma ।
[] śrī-kṛṣṇa uvāca-sa eṣa vātulatayā taralaḥ kāmaṃ jalpatu nāma, yad asabhyānām abhyākhyānam eva ca labhyam । bhavatīnām ājñā tu nāvajñātuṃ śakyate, kintu yuktam eva niyujyatām । kṛṣṇa ced bata rādhāyām udāsīno bhavān api । udāssva, kim ahaṃ tatra kaṭhora-hṛdayā bruve? ।। [anu] sātiśrīr bhavatātyāji śrīvakṣā na bhavāṃs tayā ।
vayaṃ tu saralā yugme yugmaṃ roddhuṃ na śaknumaḥ ।। [anuṣṭubh] [] kṛṣṇas tuṣṇīṃ sthitavān । [] śrī-kṛṣṇa uvāca-adharma evātra marma-bhedī bhavatīti । [] paurṇamāsī uvāca-adharmaḥ khalu mayā svīkṛta eva, dharmas tu tava vardhatām ।
[] śrī-kṛṣṇa uvāca-sparśanaṃ vinānyad anumanyatām । [] vṛndāha-darśanaṃ tāvat kriyatām । tan-mātreṇa siddha-yātre sati parama-guṇa-pātre bhavati katham anyad atha prārthayitāsmahe? dehendriya-mano-buddhi prāṇādīnāṃ priyaṃ priye । tvad-anādara-bhājo me jātaṃ sarvam anādṛtam ।।
iti rādhāṃ prati cetasi cintayantaṃ kṛṣṇam antaḥ sa-tṛṣṇam api bahis tūṣṇīkatām eva puṣṇantaṃ, madhumaṅgalaḥ kara-sarasije gṛhītvā kuṭaja-kuñja-gṛham eva nītavān । nītvā ca tat-paryanta-bhuvi vṛndāṃ rakṣitvā bāhyam avagāhya, pūrṇimāṃ saṃvāhya tasminn ante-gurutayā tatrakīyaṃ vṛttaṃ citravad īkṣitavān । indur indu-bhramaṃ yāti darpaṇaḥ pratibimbatām । mohaṃ padmālayā yatra kṛṣṇa tan-mukham īkṣyatām ।। [anuṣṭubh] tāṃ rahasi gatāṃ kisalaya-śayana-śayānām ।
harir ālokata nija-muralī-kalakalayā citrita-bhānām ।। yā nija-vadanāmṛta-rucinā tan-mukha-ratnam ajasram । bahalam asisravad iha yad bhātaṃ pratipada-sampatad asram ।। yasyā hṛdayaṃ svāntaram anu tat kāyaṃ bhaja dava-kalitam ।
bahir api taṃ pratibimba-vyājād vyānañjātmani valitam ।। yasyāṃ doṣa-trayam iti matibhiḥ prattaṃ kuṅkuma-rāgam । mene muraripur atha sākṣād iva yātaṃ hṛd-gata-rāgam ।। yāṃ paśyan sa tu sāttvika-bhāvaṃ dadhad api citta-vikāram ।
bheje yatra pratikṛti-kṛd api pratikṛtir iti ca vicāram ।। sa yayā pratikṛtitābhramam āgād evaṃ bhāvana-śālī । bhāva-parīkṣaṇa-kṛn me kṛtako' py etām indraka-jālī ।। tad api ca yatra spṛhayann atha yām enāṃ mene rādhām ।
vṛndā yācñāṃ pratyācaṣṭa ca dadhad api duḥkhād bādhām ।। sa punar yasyā hetoḥ śocan vyājita-vṛndā-vananam । vidadhe yadd hṛdi nija-pada-pallavam abhito jīvana-jananam ।। ।। । bhoga-tarṣam anumāya tan-mayam ।
svīya-śarma vijahāv iyaṃ ramā ।। [rathoddhatā] [] tad etad avadhāya bhavān apy etad-arthaṃ veṇu-vādanādikaṃ kurvann evāste, tasmād avadhānaṃ sandhāya samādhīyatām । [] vṛndāha-hastam eva hṛdi vinyastaṃ kuru । [] śrī-kṛṣṇa uvāca-tad etad atyanucitam ।
[] vṛndāha-tarhi caraṇam eva tathācara । [] śrī-kṛṣṇas tuṣṇīṃ tasthau । [] vṛndā pādayoḥ patantī-hanta, mā vilambam avalambasva iti kāku-vyākulā tayor ekaṃ balad iva tasyā hṛdi saṃvalayāmāsa । [] kṛṣṇaś ca kampa-sampadā padāravindaṃ sandadhad eva vaivaśya-vaśyatāṃ vindati sma ।
[] tataś ca sañjīvanī-pallava-vinyāsavat tal-lava-sparśata eva cakṣuḥ-puṭa-yugam udghaṭayya tayā sa eva dṛṣṭaḥ । bimba-dambham aviśat parasparam । tāv amuṣya parivṛttim aicchatām ।। [rathoddhatā] [] tadaiva sa cātrakīyāpatrapātaḥ śirasi vasanāvaraṇaḥ sahasā nirgamya pūrṇimāṃ praṇamya ca calita evāsīt । kintu skhalann iva calan, karmaṇā narmaṇā ca madhumaṅgala-dattāvalambaḥ sakhi-kulaṃ saṃvalate sma ।
[] sā ca svapnam iva paśyantī vaivaśyata eva samuttiṣṭhantī, nirakṣara-sūkṣma-rodanaṃ cānutiṣṭhantī yadā vṛndayā sādaraṃ kṛtasāntvā, tadā darasāntvā pūrṇimāṃ natvā vṛndayā saha suhṛttamekṣita-tad-āgame tasminn aparāhnetame vrajaṃ gatvā, katham api samaya-katipayān gamayāmāsa । [] yataḥ sakṛt tādṛśaṃ sukham upalabhya kṣaṇāt tad-viyuktayā tayā katham iva prathamānaṃ duḥkhaṃ stabhyatām? tat tu sukhaṃ sva-saṃvedyam eva, na tu nivedyam । tathā hi- ko vā tāṃ syāt kavayitum iha svalpakam api । aho paulindīnām api tad iva śaśvad vyatanuta ।। [śikhariṇī]
[] tad evaṃ yadā hareḥ padāravindaṃ vindamānāni kuṅkuma-paṅkāni kṛta-tad-aṅkāni pulindī-jātālaṅkāratayā jātāni, tadānīm anyāsāṃ dhanyānāṃ pūrvavad pūrvānubhava-racana-pūrvakaṃ vacanam idam, pūrṇāḥ pulindyaḥ ityādi । [] prāptaṃ tat-tṛṇam apy aho vijayatāṃ sākṣāt tu tat-saṅgi yat । yās tat prāpya nijāṅga-lepana-sukhād āsedire pūrṇatām ।। [śārdūla] sa īdṛk-praṇayī labdhas tvayā rādhe purā tu yaḥ ।
nānā-manorathaṃ cakre rathavad bhavad-āptaye ।। [anu] ।। [] atha prabhāta-kathāyāṃ prabhāta-prathāyāṃ madhukaṇṭhaḥ sphurad-utkaṇṭhas tal-līlāntaraṃ śaṃsan śaṃsad-upalabdhaṃ kartum ārabdhavān । gharmartau dhavalānikhavraśatatṛḍ-nirjiṣṇu-kṛṣṇāṃ vrajan ।
kṣud-vyājād adhiyajña-patni-karuṇā-kārī hariḥ pātu vaḥ ।। atha gopaiḥ parivṛto yaśodānanda-nandanaḥ । vṛndāvanād gato dūraṃ cārayan gāḥ sahāgrajaḥ ।।nidāghārkātape tigme cchāyābhiḥ svābhirātmanaḥ । ātapatrāyitān vīkṣya drumān mitrāṇy abhāṣata ।। []
[] tatra ca megha-nirghoṣa-nibha-gambhīratā-sambhṛta-madhura-svarata eva harṣam utkarṣayan mitra-mukhyān pratyekaṃ racitābhimukhyāṃś cakāra । yathā- he stoka-kṛṣṇa he aṃśo śrīdāman subalārjuna । viśāla rṣabha tejasvin devaprastha varūthapa ।।[] [] tata eva ca tān amṛta-kṛtābhiṣekān iva kṛtvā sa-kautukam uvāca-māṃ sukhayantu evābhimukhatas ete taravo virājante, tasmād bhavadbhir vilokya pṛthak pṛthag upaślokyantām ।
[] sarve vihasya procuḥ-bhavān evāsmāsu vismāyakatayā kavi-maṇḍalākhaṇḍala-gaṇḍa-maṇḍanam asti । tasmād ātmanaiva varṇayatu । yat tāpādi-nivāraṇaiḥ sva-vapuṣo jīvānavantaḥ sthitāḥ । ūhadhvaṃ yad aśeṣa-jīvanatayā rājanty amī sarvataḥ ।। svabhāvād viśveṣām upakṛti-vidhā dhanya-tanavaḥ ।
tato bhaktāḥ pūrve sukṛtam anu bhāktāḥ kila pare ।। [] atra vṛndāvana-vāstavyatā punar eṣāṃ stavyatām apy atikrāmati iti gūḍham abhimatam । [] sarve sa-smitam ūcuḥ-kavi-cakra-cakravartinā bhavatā na kiṃ vā supraśastaṅkaraṃ bhavitā, tato yad eva yojayiṣyate, tad eva vijeṣyate । tathā hi- vāco-yukti-paṭur yatra tvaṃ vadāvadatāṃ gataḥ ।
vācaspatiś ca tatra syān na vācaḥ-patir aṇv api ।। [] kṛṣṇo' pi sa-smitam uvāca-bhavatu, kadācid etad apy anubhaviṣyatha iti nānā-sukha-vitarakara-puruha-bhūruhāṇāṃ vanyayā mihira-kanyā-tīram udanyayā mudā jagāma । tatra ca- cātmīyāgami bhojya-vartma sa yadā santyajya kṛṣṇāṃ gataḥ । aghnyānāṃ nikaras tataḥ svayam apur gopālakās tan-mukhāḥ ।।
rāma rāma mahā-bāho kṛṣṇa duṣṭa-nibarhaṇa । ito' vidūre su-mahad vanaṃ tālāli-saṅkulam ।।[] [] ārtiś ced varivarti, tarhi nikaṭām api kuṭilayā sūratanayā-ghaṭanayā dūrāyamāṇām itas tu dakṣiṇāhi yā śūrasena-purī, tām uttareṇa niravajñaṃ yajña-śālā-mālām ālokayanta evānena samyag upatiṣṭhamānena pathā pratiṣṭhadhvam । gatvā ca tān kārmān karmaṭhācāryatamasya mama ca nāmnā yācadhvam । kintu bhikṣākāṇāṃ titikṣā-mātram ucitam iti śikṣā manasi kāryā । [] atha te' pi ke' pi saṃvalitāś calitāḥ । svayam ayaṃ tu tadīya-gatyāgati-dṛṣṭy-artham upanadaṃ mahā-kuṭṭimam adhitaṣṭhau । tataś ca-
gatyāgatyādi-ceṣṭāḥ śubha-yuta-hutabhug-vedi-bhāg-ṛtvijaś ca । yasmād brahmaṇya-deva-svatulita-suhṛdaḥ kintv idaṃ māṃ dunoti ।। [] tataś ca tān prakṛti-śleṣeṇa kenāpy ākṛti-viśleṣeṇa veṣeṇa ca gopān jñātvā vipratā-garva-parvatam ārūḍhās te tu vyūḍha-bahula-sthala-dṛṣṭayas tiṣṭhanti sma । tathāpi sakhāyas te kṛṣṇasya bubhukṣā-sukṣāmatāṃ sākṣād ivānubhūya dūyamāna-manasaḥ svayam eva nivedayāmāsuḥ । yataḥ- śabdāḥ yasmin na kvacit kṛṣṇa-mukhyāḥ ।
śrī-kṛṣṇārthaṃ kiṃ na te mānayanti ।। [] atha nivedanaṃ cedambho bho bhūmi-devāḥ ! kiñcid evāvadhānaṃ vidhīyatām । rāma-rāmānujau khalu parama-prabhāva-yujau śrutavadbhir bhavadbhir avadhāritāv eva staḥ । tau cātra bhavad-vidhānāṃ sannidhānam eva dhenu-sevanānurodhād āgatavantau । kintv adya sadya evānavadya-krīḍā-maya-śūratā-kautuka-puratas tata itaḥ saṅgatyāsannāpi pratyāsannāpi śrī-gopādhibhū-sadana-bhūr vidūrāyamāṇāsmākaṃ bhāti sma । gṛha-lokena ca na tathālocayāmbabhūvimahe । tata eva sākṣāl-lakṣmī-pati-gṛhāyamāṇa-gṛhād bhojana-saṃyojanaṃ vinā krīḍā-yudhi ca kṣudhitāv abhūtām । tataś ca kula-paramparā-prāpta-vyavahāraṃ paryāyatayā pitṛ-paryāyatayā bhavatsu saṅkocam aparyālocamānau pitṛ-bhavanād iva bhavadīya-savanād annaṃ yācitam akurvātām iti । [] atha tathāpi manasy abhakti-rasikatā-vaśikatayā tad asat-kṛtya tuṣṇīm-bhuṣṇuṣu teṣv antar-vāṇiṃ-manyeṣu tādṛg-adhanyeṣu punar amī manasi mīmāṃsayāmāsuḥ-[] nūnam asmān ete mūḍhān matvā gūḍhānubhāsaṇā babhūvus tasmād gaty-antara-racana-niṣiddha-bhāvāya siddhāntataś cāmīṣāṃ suṣṭhu mauna-biddhāntastāṃ kurma iti । [] atha spaṣṭaṃ punar ūcuḥ- prāntaṃ vijñair yājñikānnaṃ na bhojyam ।
tābhyām anyatrāsti tad grāhyam eva ।। iti । [] tatra-bhavad-bhavad-anuṣṭhāna-dṛṣṭita evāsmābhis tad-avasaraḥ sphuṭaṃ niṣṭaṅkita iti bhāvaḥ । [] tad evaṃ bhikṣā-niṣṭhānām iva tasminn upatiṣṭhamānānām api śāstrārthaṃ nayamānānāṃ tad avadhārya te vāryācāryā manasi paryālocayāmāsuḥ-hanta ! brāhmaṇā evāsmākam etān brahma-vicāram api viśiṣṭatayā lobhād anuśiṣṭavantaḥ santi । yena tatrāpi kṛta-mukhatayā mukharatām āpannāḥ । bhavatu, tathāpy ete paramebhyayopalabhyamānāḥ kiñcid dāna-rūpam avadānaṃ vinā pratyutādānāya param atrāgatāḥ । aho ! kali-praveśa-deśasya deśa-rūpam idam । [] kiṃ ca, kecic ca vipaścitas tayor īśvaratām āropayanti । tarhi bata garhitaṃ kṣudhādikaṃ katham etāvarhataḥ ?
[] tad etad vibhāvya durbhāva-bhāvatayā tathā sthiteṣu bahu-pacanatāyām api mitampaceṣu dvirjātatāyām api yathā-jāteṣu yājñika-kitavatāṃ yāteṣu teṣu yācñāyāṃ vadanānatā-kadanataḥ parasparam īkṣitvā mandaṃ mandaṃ mandākṣa-mandatayā śrī-govindam eva te vindate sma । [] govindaś ca tāṃs tathāvidhān netra-pathān vidhāya manohatān vijñāya ca hasati sma-ehi manyāmahe, yājñikebhyaḥ sva-labhyam abhyādadidhve yathā vṛkṣebhyaḥ iti । [] te' pi sa-smitam ūcuḥ-tat tu bhavanta eva jānanti, vayam api yat-preraṇa-samīraṇa-vikīrṇa-manaso jātāḥ । [] kṛṣṇas tv antar yajña-patnīnāṃ svāvaloka-prayatnānāṃ sañjānaṃs tatra cāvaśya-lābhaṃ pratijānānaḥ prahasya provāca-ā evaṃ manyadhve tarhi bhadram । mayā tu patriṇām eṣāṃ satriṇāṃ ca teṣāṃ tāratamyāvadhāraṇārtham eva tatra-bhavantaḥ prasthāpitāḥ । tataś ca-
amānināṃ yathā dharmaḥ sthitas tadvan na māninām । adyāpi cen na pratītha drāk tat-patnīḥ pratīta ca ।। [] bhavanti ca bhavanta iva yajña-patnī-janā mat-prema-mātra-sayatna-dhanāḥ । ye khalu dhṛta-mada-nava-loka-dharmaṃ dvyaha-tarṣaṃ jalaṃ pibanti, try-ahātyāsaṃ dvitra-grāsaṃ bhuñjate । [] sarve sa-vailakṣyam ācakṣata-hanta satyam evedam ।
[] kṛṣṇa uvāca-bāḍham । [] sarve sāścaryam ūcuḥ-tarhi kutukam idaṃ vidāṅkarvāma । [] iti kṛṣṇodyam anu sodyamatayā tatra tan-nimeṣata eva jigamiṣatsu teṣu sa-praṇayavatsu kṛṣṇaḥ sa-tṛṣṇam uvāca-annaṃ ca tatra śrīmad-āryādi-sahita-mad-artham arthayadhvam । [] atha punar atīva kautuka-dravataḥ parasparam atītya dravanaḥ patnī-śālāyāṃ dvija-patnīr vilokayāmāsus tābhir vilokayāmāsire ca, kṛṣṇāt prati ca iti ca niśckyire ।
varṇa-nyāsa-śubhaṃyutā kavi-jana-stavyārtha-citra-prathā । yajña-strī-kalitā kramād iha sakhīn ārdrān akārṣīn muhuḥ ।। praśasta-vetrān muralī-puraskṛtān । vilokya kṛṣṇāgam apy amaṃsata ।।
vyajijñapan vijña-varāḥ praṇamya । pūrvaṃ ca matvā na viduḥ sma kṛtyam ।। tasya prāṇa-suhṛd-varāḥ svayam amī tat-preraṇād āgatāḥ । annaṃ tatra kathaṃ kathaṃ kathaya tāḥ prāpsyanti dhairya-sthitim ।।
neyabhojya-vivṛtāv anirṇayāḥ । kṣipram ādadata vipra-subhruvaḥ ।। vividha-bhojana-bhājana-mastakāḥ । sa iti tarṣi-giraḥ paricakramuḥ ।।
vidyud vidyud-ghana-śrīḥ smita-vadana-vidhu-dyota-lakṣmī-pracāraḥ । kaṃsārātes tad āsāṃ pratipadam udabhūd bāḍham ākarṣaṇāya ।। gopakaiḥ sa viharan mudānvitaḥ । dhyānam eva gatam ity amāni ca ।।
yatra bhūsura-bhāryās taṃ sura-bhāvya-padaṃ yayuḥ । aśoka-kānanaṃ tat tu babhūvāśoka-kānanam ।। [] tataś ca tāḥ sapulaka-pulakatayā tam avalokayāmāsuḥ । kṛṣṇam apaśyan pīta-dukūlam ।
bibhratam arcitatamam arcir nava-ghana-capalāruci-mūlam ।।a।। śirasi śikhaṇḍāvalim urasi srajam api dadhataṃ giri-dhātum । indradhanur yuga-madhya-madhuratara-sandhyāṃ dhurvam atiyātum ।। udayad-aruṇa-dara-kiraṇaṃ tama iva viracita-ciratara-śobham ।
nava-kisalaya-dala-valitaṃ kaca-kulam anu kalitākhila-lobham ।। bhālopari-milad-alaka-tatiṃ śruti-kumudam udañci kapolam । smita-mukham upamita-lakṣaṇa-tārā-yuga-dhara-śaśadara-golam ।। kṛta-naṭa-veṣa-viśeṣa-vilakṣaṇa-lakṣaṇa-kṣaṇam upacita-rūpam ।
kartum ivāmṛta-vṛṣṭim uditam iha kañcana jaladhara-bhūpam ।। citraṃ tatra ca mitra-skandhārpita-bandhāvara-hastam । nirmala-kamala-vidhūnana-dakṣiṇa-dakṣiṇa-kara-ruci-śastam ।। iti । sa drāg aikṣi svayam iti gatas tat-kṛtas tāpa-vargaḥ ।
so' py āveśān milana-tulitāt tāsu na sphūrtim āpa ।। aho bata mahābhāgā yuṣmākaṃ bhūri-bhāratā । jātā saṅkocayaty asmān pṛcchadhve svāgataṃ tataḥ ।। iti । [] tad evam ehi-svāgatāṃ kriyām ācarya tat-pratyuttara-saṅkathane tāsāṃ saṅkocaṃ vicārya punar uvāca āsyatām iti ।
viśrama-kāryaṃ vilambitaṃ tanute । ajahāṃ bhavatībhir āsyatām eva ।। iti । [] tataś ca praṇaya-praṇeyatayā vikhyātaḥ so' yam āsām asaṅkocāya svayaṃ bhāram avatārayann eva samupaviśann eva ca tāḥ sadeśa eva samupaveśayāmāsa । [] punar uvāca ca-karavāma kiṃ iti ।
tad-ṛte sa tu saṅkucann āste । anujānantu tat tu bhū-devyaḥ ।। [] atha tāsām ātma-darśana-mātra-vāñchā-vimarśana-pūrvam uvāca-yan no didṛkṣayā prāptā upapannam idaṃ hi vaḥ [] iti । asmad-darśana-mātraṃ yad vo' bhīṣṭaṃ tad eva yuktaṃ ca ।
tatra hi hetur yūyaṃ tādṛśa-suṣṭhu-svabhāvāḥ stha ।। mad-viṣayā vaḥ prītiḥ kauśalyād eva nānyataḥ sacate । yan mayi kuśalāḥ sarve vīkṣyante prīti-kartāraḥ ।। mat-premāṃśād aśeṣaga-prītim ।
prīṇāty anyatra sopādhi ।। sarvatra tu mat-sphūrtir na bhavati bata sarvadeti pūrtir naḥ । bhavatīr anu sā nityā yaiva ca mat-sannidhāna-rūpaiva ।।tasmāt pati-suta-valitaṃ nilayaṃ tvarayā prayāta tā yūyam । mama ca tataḥ sukham uccaiḥ sāmañjasyaṃ hi sarvato vaśmi ।।
prāhur bhavān iva bhavān iti tat prasīda । kāraṃ nijāṅghri-parivāra-daśāṃ diśasva ।। padāmbujam upāśritāḥ paricarema taṃ tvā sadā । urīkuru puru-śravaḥ śravaṇa-maṅgala śrīpate ।।
yathā vo bāndhavā nābhyasūyeran na ca majjanāḥ । sureśāś cānumoderaṃs tathā kuruta nānyathā ।।yuṣmākaṃ vipra-bhāryāṇāṃ paricaryārtham āhṛtiḥ । kenāpi nānumodyeta pratīkṣya samayas tataḥ ।। [] tad evaṃ locana-tṛṣṇāspadāya ca kṛṣṇāya tāś cira-sthiratāṃ pratyarocamānās tasya saṅkocam ālocamānās tatra nātivilambamānās tad-ājñām ālambamānāḥ patrāmatrādiṣu bhojyaṃ saṃyojya nija-kupya-pātrāṇy ādadamānās tena sādaraṃ visarjamānāḥ sakhibhir anuvrajyamānā muhuḥ parāvṛtya tam eva vilokamānā bhṛśaṃ saṃvardhi-kṛcchraṃ kalayamānāḥ kathaṃ katham api gṛha-gatiṃ prati sacamānāḥ sva-vaṃśa-prathamānāṃ yaśaḥ-prathāṃ prathayamānā veśmāntaḥ praviśanti sma । kintu-
āśā-pūrtiṃ pratipada asāv ācarat tāsu śīghram । vāraṃ vāraṃ dṛśi vidadhatī citra-bhāvaṃ cakāra ।। anna-pātrāṇi pātrāṇi ratnānāṃ vīkṣya sakṣaṇāḥ । gṛhāṇi ca gṛhādhīśā na hīśāmāsur ūhitum ।।
bālya-krīḍā-kṛīta-phalenānena maṇi-pūritān । sva-gṛhān vīkṣya te viprāḥ sva-patnī-matim anvayuḥ ।। tasmai viśva-janīnāya yās tad-bhogīnam āharan । tā evāsann ātmanīnā dīnās tu bata mādṛśāḥ ।।
mā jīvan yasya kṛṣṇāya kramate cakṣur ādi na । mriyamāṇaś ca mā yasya tasmai tan na pravartate ।। sa kiñjīvaḥ sa kubrahmaḥ suparva-hatakaś ca saḥ । rājīva-nayanaṃ yas tu nājīvanatayā bhajet ।।
atha kṛṣṇāya tṛṣṇāṃ te dadhur vṛṣṇi-pura-dvijāḥ । kintu dhṛṣṇak kaṃsa-bhiyā nājagmuḥ kṛṣṇam īkṣitum ।। ekena kenacit pūrvaṃ bhāryāmāryātigam iva । nivārya vāryatālabdhā vāryatāyām iti śrutam ।।
kṣaṇād uccaiḥ kṣaṇān nīcair gati-bhājāṃ kanīyasām । reṇūnām iva kārmāṇāṃ viṣamā rītir īkṣyate ।। pūrvī kṛṣṇasya sevāyām iṣṭī vā tatra yaḥ sadā । adhītī vā bhāgavate bhakta-pūrvī sa taṃ bhajet ।।
[] tatra ca tair bhojya-madhurādibhir upayojyamānaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇaṃ madhumaṅgala uvāca-suṣṭhu miṣṭam idaṃ pākimatāpannam anna-jātaṃ yācita kam apy amṛtāyate । nedṛśam āpam ity akam amṛtaṃ vā । yat khalu bhūmi-skhalitaṃ sarajasaṃ kaṇam apy abhyavahartum īhāmahe । tasmād asmākam eva parṇaśālābhyarṇe tāḥ kuṭīr vidhāya tiṣṭhantu, tat-kṛta-madhura-paripāka-pāka-śāka-sūpa-pūpa-pūṭīs tu savayaso vayam eva yuṣmabhyam uṣṇāḥ koṣṇā eva samarpayiṣyāmaḥ । tatrāpy āha prāgraharatayā prāgrahara eva bhaviṣyāmīti sthite ko vāyaṃ doṣaḥ । kintu roṣa-bhiyā na vaktuṃ śaktāḥ sma । [] kṛṣṇa uvāca-ādyūna nūnam unmadiṣṇutayāpatra-piṣṇutām apy aticariṣṇur jāto' si । [] atha sarve' pi hasantaḥ procuḥ-priya-vayasya ! yady apy asau parānnatārocanam āpannas tarhi sa eṣa eva tundaparimṛja iva vipra-sundarīṇāṃ tāsām upāsanāṃ ghaṭayamānas tad-bāṭa-taṭagam uṭajam adhitiṣṭhan sambhavad āśitambhavān miṣṭam iṣṭa-vighasa-bhojanān nijam iṣṭaṃ racayatu । [] kṛṣṇa uvāca-sādhūktaṃ vyaktam idaṃ bhagavatī-viditaṃ vidhāsyāmaḥ ।
[] madhumaṅgalas tu sa-krodham ivovāca-yuvarāja ! gardhanatayā kukṣim-bharayas te eta eva muhur aśanāyāṃ smarayantaḥ sarvatra ca ghasmarā eva bhaṇyante, bhikṣāyām akṣāma-samudyamatayā sarvānnīnāś ca lakṣyante, na tu vayam । [] sarve' py ūcuḥ-vāvadūka ! vipratayā bhavān eva yāyajūkatāyāṃ jañjapūkatām āsīdan purobhāśānāṃ dandaśūkas tad-āsvādāya jāgarūkatām āsādayati । asmābhis tu bhavaj-jāter dvijāteḥ parīkṣaivācaritā iti । [] tad evaṃ hasatsu sakhi-sabhāsatsu svayam āśitambhavenodana-sambhāreṇa bhuktvā suhitaḥ sarva-hitaḥ śrāvita-veṇur dhenuḥ prāpya tat-tat-kathā-kautukatas tad-artham anugavam āsādita-dṛṣṭi-vrajaṃ śrīmad-vrajam avāpya nija-viraha-dahanaṃ nirvāpya svaka-rūpāmṛtenāpyāyayāmāsa । [] sakhāyas tu yājñikeṣu jagmivāṃso jakṣivāṃsaś ca vayam iti saṅkocena na kañcid apy ūcivāṃsaś ca ।
।। MISSING! so' yaṃ śrī-gokulādhīśa kulādhīśas tavoditaḥ । ākarṣaṇād guṇā yasya sarvān anuguṇān vyadhuḥ ।। ।।
